-- 10001 //위암 환자수
INSERT INTO CNCR_TBL_SMRY_STATS
(SMRY_STATS_NO, HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, SMRY_STATS_NM, TBL_ID, COL_ID, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, NCS, WHOL_NCS, PT_CNT, WHOL_PT_CNT, STATS_WORK_YMD, COLL_STRT_YMD, COLL_END_YMD, CRTN_DT) 
WITH W1 AS (
SELECT HCODE AS HOSP_CD, PTNO AS PT_SBST_NO, SUBSTRING(FDX,1,4) AS CRIT_YR,  
CASE WHEN AGE<'20' THEN 10 --20세 미만
     WHEN AGE<'30' THEN 20  --20대
     WHEN AGE<'40' THEN 30  --30대
     WHEN AGE<'50' THEN 40  --40대 
     WHEN AGE<'60' THEN 50  --50대
     WHEN AGE<'70' THEN 60  --60대
     WHEN AGE<'80' THEN 70  --70대
     WHEN AGE>='80' THEN 80  --80대 이상 
   END AS PT_AGE,
SEX AS PT_SEX_CD, POPCODE AS STATS_TRGT_VL
FROM (SELECT DISTINCT HCODE, PTNO, MIN(AGE) AS AGE, SEX, MIN(FDX) AS FDX, POPCODE FROM CNCR_RGST WHERE POPCODE = '04' GROUP BY HCODE, PTNO,SEX, POPCODE) A -- '04' 위암
WHERE FDX BETWEEN '20100101' AND '20211231'
)
SELECT 10001 AS SMRY_STATS_NO, A.HOSP_CD, A.CRIT_YR, '위암 환자수' AS SMRY_STATS_NM, 99010 AS TBL_ID, 9901002 AS COL_ID,
cast(A.PT_AGE as INTEGER) as PT_AGE, A.PT_SEX_CD, A.STATS_TRGT_VL, A.NCS,  B.WHOL_NCS, A.PT_CNT, B.WHOL_PT_CNT, 
TO_CHAR(CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,'YYYYMMDD') AS STATS_WORK_YMD, '20100101' AS COLL_STRT_YMD, '20211231' AS COLL_END_YMD, CURRENT_TIMESTAMP AS CRTN_DT FROM 
(SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL) AS A 
INNER JOIN (SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS WHOL_NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  WHOL_PT_CNT 
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) AS B 
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=B.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = B.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = B.PT_SEX_CD;


-- 10002 //위암 음주여부별

INSERT INTO CNCR_TBL_SMRY_STATS
(SMRY_STATS_NO, HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, SMRY_STATS_NM, TBL_ID, COL_ID, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, NCS, WHOL_NCS, PT_CNT, WHOL_PT_CNT, STATS_WORK_YMD, COLL_STRT_YMD, COLL_END_YMD, CRTN_DT) 
WITH W1 AS (
SELECT A.HOSP_CD, A.PT_SBST_NO, SUBSTRING(A.ADM_YMD,1,4) AS CRIT_YR,  
CASE WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ADM_YMD)/365.25) <'20' THEN 10 --20세 미만
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ADM_YMD)/365.25) <'30' THEN 20  --20대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ADM_YMD)/365.25) <'40' THEN 30  --30대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ADM_YMD)/365.25) <'50' THEN 40  --40대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ADM_YMD)/365.25) <'60' THEN 50  --50대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ADM_YMD)/365.25) <'70' THEN 60  --60대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ADM_YMD)/365.25) <'80' THEN 70  --70대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ADM_YMD)/365.25)  >='80' THEN 80  --80대 이상
   END AS PT_AGE,
B.SEX AS PT_SEX_CD, A.CUR_DRNK_YN_NOANS_SPCD as STATS_TRGT_COL, 
ifnull(A.CUR_DRNK_YN_NOANS_SPCD,'#N/A' ) AS STATS_TRGT_VL -- NULL은 '#N/A'로 대체
FROM GSCN_PT_HLINF A
INNER JOIN (SELECT DISTINCT HCODE, PTNO, ADD_DAYS(BRTH, 14) AS BRTH, SEX FROM CNCR_RGST WHERE BRTH IS NOT NULL AND POPCODE = '04' ) B -- '04' 위암
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HCODE
AND A.PT_SBST_NO = B.PTNO
AND A.ADM_YMD BETWEEN '20100101' AND '20211231'
) 
SELECT 10002 AS SMRY_STATS_NO, A.HOSP_CD, A.CRIT_YR, '위암 음주여부별' AS SMRY_STATS_NM, 10010 AS TBL_ID, 1001006 AS COL_ID,
cast(A.PT_AGE as INTEGER) as PT_AGE, A.PT_SEX_CD, A.STATS_TRGT_VL, A.NCS,  B.WHOL_NCS, A.PT_CNT, B.WHOL_PT_CNT, 
TO_CHAR(CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,'YYYYMMDD') AS STATS_WORK_YMD, '20100101' AS COLL_STRT_YMD, '20211231' AS COLL_END_YMD, CURRENT_TIMESTAMP AS CRTN_DT FROM 
(SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL) AS A  
INNER JOIN (SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS WHOL_NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  WHOL_PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) AS B  
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=B.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = B.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = B.PT_SEX_CD  
INNER JOIN (select HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, count(STATS_TRGT_COL) as STATS_TRGT_CNT from w1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) C  
ON A.HOSP_CD = C.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=C.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = C.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = C.PT_SEX_CD where C.STATS_TRGT_CNT <> 0;


-- 10003 //위암 음주력여부별

INSERT INTO CNCR_TBL_SMRY_STATS
(SMRY_STATS_NO, HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, SMRY_STATS_NM, TBL_ID, COL_ID, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, NCS, WHOL_NCS, PT_CNT, WHOL_PT_CNT, STATS_WORK_YMD, COLL_STRT_YMD, COLL_END_YMD, CRTN_DT) 
WITH W1 AS (
SELECT A.HOSP_CD, A.PT_SBST_NO, SUBSTRING(A.ADM_YMD,1,4) AS CRIT_YR,  
CASE WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ADM_YMD)/365.25) <'20' THEN 10 --20세 미만
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ADM_YMD)/365.25) <'30' THEN 20  --20대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ADM_YMD)/365.25) <'40' THEN 30  --30대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ADM_YMD)/365.25) <'50' THEN 40  --40대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ADM_YMD)/365.25) <'60' THEN 50  --50대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ADM_YMD)/365.25) <'70' THEN 60  --60대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ADM_YMD)/365.25) <'80' THEN 70  --70대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ADM_YMD)/365.25)  >='80' THEN 80  --80대 이상
   END AS PT_AGE,
B.SEX AS PT_SEX_CD, A.DHIS_YN_NOANS_SPCD as STATS_TRGT_COL, 
ifnull(A.DHIS_YN_NOANS_SPCD,'#N/A' ) AS STATS_TRGT_VL -- NULL은 '#N/A'로 대체
FROM GSCN_PT_HLINF A
INNER JOIN (SELECT DISTINCT HCODE, PTNO, ADD_DAYS(BRTH, 14) AS BRTH, SEX FROM CNCR_RGST WHERE BRTH IS NOT NULL AND POPCODE = '04' ) B -- '04' 위암
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HCODE
AND A.PT_SBST_NO = B.PTNO
AND A.ADM_YMD BETWEEN '20100101' AND '20211231'
) 
SELECT 10003 AS SMRY_STATS_NO, A.HOSP_CD, A.CRIT_YR, '위암 음주력여부별' AS SMRY_STATS_NM, 10010 AS TBL_ID, 1001008 AS COL_ID,
cast(A.PT_AGE as INTEGER) as PT_AGE, A.PT_SEX_CD, A.STATS_TRGT_VL, A.NCS,  B.WHOL_NCS, A.PT_CNT, B.WHOL_PT_CNT, 
TO_CHAR(CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,'YYYYMMDD') AS STATS_WORK_YMD, '20100101' AS COLL_STRT_YMD, '20211231' AS COLL_END_YMD, CURRENT_TIMESTAMP AS CRTN_DT FROM 
(SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL) AS A  
INNER JOIN (SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS WHOL_NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  WHOL_PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) AS B  
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=B.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = B.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = B.PT_SEX_CD  
INNER JOIN (select HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, count(STATS_TRGT_COL) as STATS_TRGT_CNT from w1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) C  
ON A.HOSP_CD = C.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=C.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = C.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = C.PT_SEX_CD where C.STATS_TRGT_CNT <> 0;

-- 10007 //위암 음주횟수별

INSERT INTO CNCR_TBL_SMRY_STATS
(SMRY_STATS_NO, HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, SMRY_STATS_NM, TBL_ID, COL_ID, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, NCS, WHOL_NCS, PT_CNT, WHOL_PT_CNT, STATS_WORK_YMD, COLL_STRT_YMD, COLL_END_YMD, CRTN_DT) 
WITH W1 AS (
SELECT A.HOSP_CD, A.PT_SBST_NO, SUBSTRING(A.ADM_YMD,1,4) AS CRIT_YR,  
CASE WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ADM_YMD)/365.25) <'20' THEN 10 --20세 미만
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ADM_YMD)/365.25) <'30' THEN 20  --20대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ADM_YMD)/365.25) <'40' THEN 30  --30대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ADM_YMD)/365.25) <'50' THEN 40  --40대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ADM_YMD)/365.25) <'60' THEN 50  --50대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ADM_YMD)/365.25) <'70' THEN 60  --60대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ADM_YMD)/365.25) <'80' THEN 70  --70대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ADM_YMD)/365.25)  >='80' THEN 80  --80대 이상
   END AS PT_AGE,
B.SEX AS PT_SEX_CD, A.DRNK_NT as STATS_TRGT_COL, 
ifnull(A.DRNK_NT,'#N/A' ) AS STATS_TRGT_VL -- NULL은 '#N/A'로 대체
FROM GSCN_PT_HLINF A
INNER JOIN (SELECT DISTINCT HCODE, PTNO, ADD_DAYS(BRTH, 14) AS BRTH, SEX FROM CNCR_RGST WHERE BRTH IS NOT NULL AND POPCODE = '04' ) B -- '04' 위암
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HCODE
AND A.PT_SBST_NO = B.PTNO
AND A.ADM_YMD BETWEEN '20100101' AND '20211231'
) 
SELECT 10007 AS SMRY_STATS_NO, A.HOSP_CD, A.CRIT_YR, '위암 음주횟수별' AS SMRY_STATS_NM, 10010 AS TBL_ID, 1001014 AS COL_ID,
cast(A.PT_AGE as INTEGER) as PT_AGE, A.PT_SEX_CD, A.STATS_TRGT_VL, A.NCS,  B.WHOL_NCS, A.PT_CNT, B.WHOL_PT_CNT, 
TO_CHAR(CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,'YYYYMMDD') AS STATS_WORK_YMD, '20100101' AS COLL_STRT_YMD, '20211231' AS COLL_END_YMD, CURRENT_TIMESTAMP AS CRTN_DT FROM 
(SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL) AS A  
INNER JOIN (SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS WHOL_NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  WHOL_PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) AS B  
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=B.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = B.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = B.PT_SEX_CD  
INNER JOIN (select HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, count(STATS_TRGT_COL) as STATS_TRGT_CNT from w1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) C  
ON A.HOSP_CD = C.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=C.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = C.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = C.PT_SEX_CD where C.STATS_TRGT_CNT <> 0;

(SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL) AS A  
INNER JOIN (SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS WHOL_NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  WHOL_PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) AS B  
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=B.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = B.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = B.PT_SEX_CD  
INNER JOIN (select HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, count(STATS_TRGT_COL) as STATS_TRGT_CNT from w1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) C  
ON A.HOSP_CD = C.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=C.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = C.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = C.PT_SEX_CD where C.STATS_TRGT_CNT <> 0;


-- 10013 //위암 흡연기간년수별

INSERT INTO CNCR_TBL_SMRY_STATS
(SMRY_STATS_NO, HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, SMRY_STATS_NM, TBL_ID, COL_ID, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, NCS, WHOL_NCS, PT_CNT, WHOL_PT_CNT, STATS_WORK_YMD, COLL_STRT_YMD, COLL_END_YMD, CRTN_DT) 
WITH W1 AS (
SELECT A.HOSP_CD, A.PT_SBST_NO, SUBSTRING(A.ADM_YMD,1,4) AS CRIT_YR,  
CASE WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ADM_YMD)/365.25) <'20' THEN 10 --20세 미만
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ADM_YMD)/365.25) <'30' THEN 20  --20대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ADM_YMD)/365.25) <'40' THEN 30  --30대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ADM_YMD)/365.25) <'50' THEN 40  --40대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ADM_YMD)/365.25) <'60' THEN 50  --50대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ADM_YMD)/365.25) <'70' THEN 60  --60대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ADM_YMD)/365.25) <'80' THEN 70  --70대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ADM_YMD)/365.25)  >='80' THEN 80  --80대 이상
   END AS PT_AGE,
B.SEX AS PT_SEX_CD, A.SMOK_DTRN_YCNT as STATS_TRGT_COL, 
ifnull(A.SMOK_DTRN_YCNT,'#N/A' ) AS STATS_TRGT_VL -- NULL은 '#N/A'로 대체
FROM GSCN_PT_HLINF A
INNER JOIN (SELECT DISTINCT HCODE, PTNO, ADD_DAYS(BRTH, 14) AS BRTH, SEX FROM CNCR_RGST WHERE BRTH IS NOT NULL AND POPCODE = '04' ) B -- '04' 위암
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HCODE
AND A.PT_SBST_NO = B.PTNO
AND A.ADM_YMD BETWEEN '20100101' AND '20211231'
) 
SELECT 10013 AS SMRY_STATS_NO, A.HOSP_CD, A.CRIT_YR, '위암 흡연기간년수별' AS SMRY_STATS_NM, 10010 AS TBL_ID, 1001022 AS COL_ID,

TO_CHAR(CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,'YYYYMMDD') AS STATS_WORK_YMD, '20100101' AS COLL_STRT_YMD, '20211231' AS COLL_END_YMD, CURRENT_TIMESTAMP AS CRTN_DT FROM 
(SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  PT_CNT

ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=B.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = B.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = B.PT_SEX_CD

     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ADM_YMD)/365.25) <'70' THEN 60  --60대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ADM_YMD)/365.25) <'80' THEN 70  --70대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ADM_YMD)/365.25)  >='80' THEN 80  --80대 이상
   END AS PT_AGE,
B.SEX AS PT_SEX_CD, A.MHIS_HTN_YN_NOANS_SPCD as STATS_TRGT_COL, 
ifnull(A.MHIS_HTN_YN_NOANS_SPCD,'#N/A' ) AS STATS_TRGT_VL -- NULL은 '#N/A'로 대체
FROM GSCN_PT_HLINF A
INNER JOIN (SELECT DISTINCT HCODE, PTNO, ADD_DAYS(BRTH, 14) AS BRTH, SEX FROM CNCR_RGST WHERE BRTH IS NOT NULL AND POPCODE = '04' ) B -- '04' 위암
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HCODE
AND A.PT_SBST_NO = B.PTNO
AND A.ADM_YMD BETWEEN '20100101' AND '20211231'
) 
SELECT 10018 AS SMRY_STATS_NO, A.HOSP_CD, A.CRIT_YR, '위암 병력고혈압여부별' AS SMRY_STATS_NM, 10010 AS TBL_ID, 1001029 AS COL_ID,
cast(A.PT_AGE as INTEGER) as PT_AGE, A.PT_SEX_CD, A.STATS_TRGT_VL, A.NCS,  B.WHOL_NCS, A.PT_CNT, B.WHOL_PT_CNT, 
TO_CHAR(CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,'YYYYMMDD') AS STATS_WORK_YMD, '20100101' AS COLL_STRT_YMD, '20211231' AS COLL_END_YMD, CURRENT_TIMESTAMP AS CRTN_DT FROM 
(SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL) AS A  
INNER JOIN (SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS WHOL_NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  WHOL_PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) AS B  
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=B.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = B.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = B.PT_SEX_CD  
INNER JOIN (select HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, count(STATS_TRGT_COL) as STATS_TRGT_CNT from w1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) C  
ON A.HOSP_CD = C.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=C.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = C.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = C.PT_SEX_CD where C.STATS_TRGT_CNT <> 0;

INNER JOIN (select HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, count(STATS_TRGT_COL) as STATS_TRGT_CNT from w1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) C  
ON A.HOSP_CD = C.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=C.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = C.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = C.PT_SEX_CD where C.STATS_TRGT_CNT <> 0;


-- 10024 //위암 병력우울증여부별

INSERT INTO CNCR_TBL_SMRY_STATS
(SMRY_STATS_NO, HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, SMRY_STATS_NM, TBL_ID, COL_ID, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, NCS, WHOL_NCS, PT_CNT, WHOL_PT_CNT, STATS_WORK_YMD, COLL_STRT_YMD, COLL_END_YMD, CRTN_DT) 
WITH W1 AS (
SELECT A.HOSP_CD, A.PT_SBST_NO, SUBSTRING(A.ADM_YMD,1,4) AS CRIT_YR,  
CASE WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ADM_YMD)/365.25) <'20' THEN 10 --20세 미만
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ADM_YMD)/365.25) <'30' THEN 20  --20대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ADM_YMD)/365.25) <'40' THEN 30  --30대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ADM_YMD)/365.25) <'50' THEN 40  --40대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ADM_YMD)/365.25) <'60' THEN 50  --50대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ADM_YMD)/365.25) <'70' THEN 60  --60대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ADM_YMD)/365.25) <'80' THEN 70  --70대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ADM_YMD)/365.25)  >='80' THEN 80  --80대 이상
   END AS PT_AGE,
B.SEX AS PT_SEX_CD, A.MHIS_DEPR_YN_NOANS_SPCD as STATS_TRGT_COL, 
ifnull(A.MHIS_DEPR_YN_NOANS_SPCD,'#N/A' ) AS STATS_TRGT_VL -- NULL은 '#N/A'로 대체
FROM GSCN_PT_HLINF A
INNER JOIN (SELECT DISTINCT HCODE, PTNO, ADD_DAYS(BRTH, 14) AS BRTH, SEX FROM CNCR_RGST WHERE BRTH IS NOT NULL AND POPCODE = '04' ) B -- '04' 위암
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HCODE
AND A.PT_SBST_NO = B.PTNO
AND A.ADM_YMD BETWEEN '20100101' AND '20211231'
) 
SELECT 10024 AS SMRY_STATS_NO, A.HOSP_CD, A.CRIT_YR, '위암 병력우울증여부별' AS SMRY_STATS_NM, 10010 AS TBL_ID, 1001041 AS COL_ID,
cast(A.PT_AGE as INTEGER) as PT_AGE, A.PT_SEX_CD, A.STATS_TRGT_VL, A.NCS,  B.WHOL_NCS, A.PT_CNT, B.WHOL_PT_CNT, 
TO_CHAR(CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,'YYYYMMDD') AS STATS_WORK_YMD, '20100101' AS COLL_STRT_YMD, '20211231' AS COLL_END_YMD, CURRENT_TIMESTAMP AS CRTN_DT FROM 
(SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL) AS A  
INNER JOIN (SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS WHOL_NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  WHOL_PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) AS B  
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=B.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = B.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = B.PT_SEX_CD  
INNER JOIN (select HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, count(STATS_TRGT_COL) as STATS_TRGT_CNT from w1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) C  
ON A.HOSP_CD = C.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=C.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = C.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = C.PT_SEX_CD where C.STATS_TRGT_CNT <> 0;

INNER JOIN (SELECT DISTINCT HCODE, PTNO, ADD_DAYS(BRTH, 14) AS BRTH, SEX FROM CNCR_RGST WHERE BRTH IS NOT NULL AND POPCODE = '04' ) B -- '04' 위암
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HCODE
AND A.PT_SBST_NO = B.PTNO
AND A.ADM_YMD BETWEEN '20100101' AND '20211231'
) 
SELECT 10031 AS SMRY_STATS_NO, A.HOSP_CD, A.CRIT_YR, '위암 타병원진단후전원여부별' AS SMRY_STATS_NM, 10010 AS TBL_ID, 1001053 AS COL_ID,
cast(A.PT_AGE as INTEGER) as PT_AGE, A.PT_SEX_CD, A.STATS_TRGT_VL, A.NCS,  B.WHOL_NCS, A.PT_CNT, B.WHOL_PT_CNT, 
TO_CHAR(CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,'YYYYMMDD') AS STATS_WORK_YMD, '20100101' AS COLL_STRT_YMD, '20211231' AS COLL_END_YMD, CURRENT_TIMESTAMP AS CRTN_DT FROM 
(SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL) AS A  
INNER JOIN (SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS WHOL_NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  WHOL_PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) AS B  
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=B.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = B.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = B.PT_SEX_CD  
INNER JOIN (select HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, count(STATS_TRGT_COL) as STATS_TRGT_CNT from w1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) C  
ON A.HOSP_CD = C.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=C.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = C.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = C.PT_SEX_CD where C.STATS_TRGT_CNT <> 0;

     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ADM_YMD)/365.25) <'30' THEN 20  --20대

     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ADM_YMD)/365.25) <'70' THEN 60  --60대

     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ADM_YMD)/365.25)  >='80' THEN 80  --80대 이상
   END AS PT_AGE,

ifnull(A.DSCH_STCD,'#N/A' ) AS STATS_TRGT_VL -- NULL은 '#N/A'로 대체

-- 10038 //위암 가족력결핵여부별

INSERT INTO CNCR_TBL_SMRY_STATS
(SMRY_STATS_NO, HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, SMRY_STATS_NM, TBL_ID, COL_ID, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, NCS, WHOL_NCS, PT_CNT, WHOL_PT_CNT, STATS_WORK_YMD, COLL_STRT_YMD, COLL_END_YMD, CRTN_DT) 
WITH W1 AS (
SELECT A.HOSP_CD, A.PT_SBST_NO, SUBSTRING(A.FMHT_RCRD_YMD,1,4) AS CRIT_YR,  
CASE WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.FMHT_RCRD_YMD)/365.25) <'20' THEN 10 --20세 미만
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.FMHT_RCRD_YMD)/365.25) <'30' THEN 20  --20대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.FMHT_RCRD_YMD)/365.25) <'40' THEN 30  --30대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.FMHT_RCRD_YMD)/365.25) <'50' THEN 40  --40대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.FMHT_RCRD_YMD)/365.25) <'60' THEN 50  --50대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.FMHT_RCRD_YMD)/365.25) <'70' THEN 60  --60대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.FMHT_RCRD_YMD)/365.25) <'80' THEN 70  --70대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.FMHT_RCRD_YMD)/365.25)  >='80' THEN 80  --80대 이상
   END AS PT_AGE,
B.SEX AS PT_SEX_CD, A.FMHT_TB_YN_NOANS_SPCD as STATS_TRGT_COL, 
ifnull(A.FMHT_TB_YN_NOANS_SPCD,'#N/A' ) AS STATS_TRGT_VL -- NULL은 '#N/A'로 대체
FROM GSCN_PT_FMHT A
INNER JOIN (SELECT DISTINCT HCODE, PTNO, ADD_DAYS(BRTH, 14) AS BRTH, SEX FROM CNCR_RGST WHERE BRTH IS NOT NULL AND POPCODE = '04' ) B -- '04' 위암
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HCODE
AND A.PT_SBST_NO = B.PTNO
AND A.FMHT_RCRD_YMD BETWEEN '20100101' AND '20211231'
) 
SELECT 10038 AS SMRY_STATS_NO, A.HOSP_CD, A.CRIT_YR, '위암 가족력결핵여부별' AS SMRY_STATS_NM, 10020 AS TBL_ID, 1002014 AS COL_ID,
cast(A.PT_AGE as INTEGER) as PT_AGE, A.PT_SEX_CD, A.STATS_TRGT_VL, A.NCS,  B.WHOL_NCS, A.PT_CNT, B.WHOL_PT_CNT, 
TO_CHAR(CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,'YYYYMMDD') AS STATS_WORK_YMD, '20100101' AS COLL_STRT_YMD, '20211231' AS COLL_END_YMD, CURRENT_TIMESTAMP AS CRTN_DT FROM 
(SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL) AS A  
INNER JOIN (SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS WHOL_NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  WHOL_PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) AS B  
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=B.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = B.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = B.PT_SEX_CD  
INNER JOIN (select HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, count(STATS_TRGT_COL) as STATS_TRGT_CNT from w1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) C  
ON A.HOSP_CD = C.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=C.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = C.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = C.PT_SEX_CD where C.STATS_TRGT_CNT <> 0;

     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ANTH_RCRD_YMD)/365.25) <'80' THEN 70  --70대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ANTH_RCRD_YMD)/365.25)  >='80' THEN 80  --80대 이상
   END AS PT_AGE,
B.SEX AS PT_SEX_CD, A.WT_MSRM_VL as STATS_TRGT_COL, 
ifnull(TO_CHAR(A.WT_MSRM_VL),'#N/A' ) AS STATS_TRGT_VL -- NUMERIC 컬럼 변환(NULL은 '#N/A'로 대체)
FROM GSCN_DIAG_ANINF A
INNER JOIN (SELECT DISTINCT HCODE, PTNO, ADD_DAYS(BRTH, 14) AS BRTH, SEX FROM CNCR_RGST WHERE BRTH IS NOT NULL AND POPCODE = '04' ) B -- '04'위암
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HCODE
AND A.PT_SBST_NO = B.PTNO
AND A.ANTH_RCRD_YMD BETWEEN '20100101' AND '20211231'
) 
SELECT 10046 AS SMRY_STATS_NO, A.HOSP_CD, A.CRIT_YR, '위암 체중측정별' AS SMRY_STATS_NM, 10030 AS TBL_ID, 1003006 AS COL_ID,
cast(A.PT_AGE as INTEGER) as PT_AGE, A.PT_SEX_CD, A.STATS_TRGT_VL, A.NCS,  B.WHOL_NCS, A.PT_CNT, B.WHOL_PT_CNT, 
TO_CHAR(CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,'YYYYMMDD') AS STATS_WORK_YMD, '20100101' AS COLL_STRT_YMD, '20211231' AS COLL_END_YMD, CURRENT_TIMESTAMP AS CRTN_DT FROM 
(SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL) AS A  
INNER JOIN (SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS WHOL_NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  WHOL_PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) AS B  
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=B.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = B.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = B.PT_SEX_CD  
INNER JOIN (select HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, count(STATS_TRGT_COL) as STATS_TRGT_CNT from w1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) C  
ON A.HOSP_CD = C.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=C.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = C.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = C.PT_SEX_CD where C.STATS_TRGT_CNT <> 0;

INNER JOIN (select HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, count(STATS_TRGT_COL) as STATS_TRGT_CNT from w1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) C  
ON A.HOSP_CD = C.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=C.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = C.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = C.PT_SEX_CD where C.STATS_TRGT_CNT <> 0;


-- 10219 //위암 진단KCD코드별

INSERT INTO CNCR_TBL_SMRY_STATS
(SMRY_STATS_NO, HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, SMRY_STATS_NM, TBL_ID, COL_ID, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, NCS, WHOL_NCS, PT_CNT, WHOL_PT_CNT, STATS_WORK_YMD, COLL_STRT_YMD, COLL_END_YMD, CRTN_DT) 
WITH W1 AS (
SELECT A.HOSP_CD, A.PT_SBST_NO, SUBSTRING(A.DIAG_RGST_YMD,1,4) AS CRIT_YR,  
CASE WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.DIAG_RGST_YMD)/365.25) <'20' THEN 10 --20세 미만
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.DIAG_RGST_YMD)/365.25) <'30' THEN 20  --20대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.DIAG_RGST_YMD)/365.25) <'40' THEN 30  --30대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.DIAG_RGST_YMD)/365.25) <'50' THEN 40  --40대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.DIAG_RGST_YMD)/365.25) <'60' THEN 50  --50대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.DIAG_RGST_YMD)/365.25) <'70' THEN 60  --60대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.DIAG_RGST_YMD)/365.25) <'80' THEN 70  --70대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.DIAG_RGST_YMD)/365.25)  >='80' THEN 80  --80대 이상
   END AS PT_AGE,
B.SEX AS PT_SEX_CD, A.DIAG_KCD_CD as STATS_TRGT_COL, 
ifnull(A.DIAG_KCD_CD,'#N/A' ) AS STATS_TRGT_VL -- NULL은 '#N/A'로 대체
FROM GSCN_DIAG_INF A
INNER JOIN (SELECT DISTINCT HCODE, PTNO, ADD_DAYS(BRTH, 14) AS BRTH, SEX FROM CNCR_RGST WHERE BRTH IS NOT NULL AND POPCODE = '04' ) B -- '04' 위암
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HCODE
AND A.PT_SBST_NO = B.PTNO
AND A.DIAG_RGST_YMD BETWEEN '20100101' AND '20211231'
) 
SELECT 10219 AS SMRY_STATS_NO, A.HOSP_CD, A.CRIT_YR, '위암 진단KCD코드별' AS SMRY_STATS_NM, 10040 AS TBL_ID, 1004009 AS COL_ID,
cast(A.PT_AGE as INTEGER) as PT_AGE, A.PT_SEX_CD, A.STATS_TRGT_VL, A.NCS,  B.WHOL_NCS, A.PT_CNT, B.WHOL_PT_CNT, 
TO_CHAR(CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,'YYYYMMDD') AS STATS_WORK_YMD, '20100101' AS COLL_STRT_YMD, '20211231' AS COLL_END_YMD, CURRENT_TIMESTAMP AS CRTN_DT FROM 
(SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL) AS A  
INNER JOIN (SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS WHOL_NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  WHOL_PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) AS B  
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=B.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = B.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = B.PT_SEX_CD  
INNER JOIN (select HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, count(STATS_TRGT_COL) as STATS_TRGT_CNT from w1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) C

     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.DIAG_STAG_RCRD_YMD)/365.25) <'80' THEN 70  --70대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.DIAG_STAG_RCRD_YMD)/365.25)  >='80' THEN 80  --80대 이상
   END AS PT_AGE,
B.SEX AS PT_SEX_CD, A.CLNC_TNM_STAG_VL as STATS_TRGT_COL, 
ifnull(A.CLNC_TNM_STAG_VL,'#N/A' ) AS STATS_TRGT_VL -- NULL은 '#N/A'로 대체
FROM GSCN_DIAG_STAG A
INNER JOIN (SELECT DISTINCT HCODE, PTNO, ADD_DAYS(BRTH, 14) AS BRTH, SEX FROM CNCR_RGST WHERE BRTH IS NOT NULL AND POPCODE = '04' ) B -- '04' 위암
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HCODE
AND A.PT_SBST_NO = B.PTNO
AND A.DIAG_STAG_RCRD_YMD BETWEEN '20100101' AND '20211231'
) 
SELECT 10056 AS SMRY_STATS_NO, A.HOSP_CD, A.CRIT_YR, '위암 임상TNM병기별' AS SMRY_STATS_NM, 10050 AS TBL_ID, 1005008 AS COL_ID,
cast(A.PT_AGE as INTEGER) as PT_AGE, A.PT_SEX_CD, A.STATS_TRGT_VL, A.NCS,  B.WHOL_NCS, A.PT_CNT, B.WHOL_PT_CNT, 
TO_CHAR(CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,'YYYYMMDD') AS STATS_WORK_YMD, '20100101' AS COLL_STRT_YMD, '20211231' AS COLL_END_YMD, CURRENT_TIMESTAMP AS CRTN_DT FROM 
(SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL) AS A  
INNER JOIN (SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS WHOL_NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  WHOL_PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) AS B  
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=B.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = B.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = B.PT_SEX_CD  
INNER JOIN (select HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, count(STATS_TRGT_COL) as STATS_TRGT_CNT from w1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) C  
ON A.HOSP_CD = C.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=C.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = C.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = C.PT_SEX_CD where C.STATS_TRGT_CNT <> 0;

FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) AS B  
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=B.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = B.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = B.PT_SEX_CD  
INNER JOIN (select HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, count(STATS_TRGT_COL) as STATS_TRGT_CNT from w1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) C  
ON A.HOSP_CD = C.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=C.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = C.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = C.PT_SEX_CD where C.STATS_TRGT_CNT <> 0;


-- 10062 //위암 전이양상별

INSERT INTO CNCR_TBL_SMRY_STATS
(SMRY_STATS_NO, HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, SMRY_STATS_NM, TBL_ID, COL_ID, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, NCS, WHOL_NCS, PT_CNT, WHOL_PT_CNT, STATS_WORK_YMD, COLL_STRT_YMD, COLL_END_YMD, CRTN_DT) 
WITH W1 AS (
SELECT A.HOSP_CD, A.PT_SBST_NO, SUBSTRING(A.MTDG_YMD,1,4) AS CRIT_YR,  
CASE WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.MTDG_YMD)/365.25) <'20' THEN 10 --20세 미만
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.MTDG_YMD)/365.25) <'30' THEN 20  --20대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.MTDG_YMD)/365.25) <'40' THEN 30  --30대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.MTDG_YMD)/365.25) <'50' THEN 40  --40대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.MTDG_YMD)/365.25) <'60' THEN 50  --50대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.MTDG_YMD)/365.25) <'70' THEN 60  --60대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.MTDG_YMD)/365.25) <'80' THEN 70  --70대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.MTDG_YMD)/365.25)  >='80' THEN 80  --80대 이상
   END AS PT_AGE,
B.SEX AS PT_SEX_CD, A.MTST_ASPT_CD as STATS_TRGT_COL, 
ifnull(A.MTST_ASPT_CD,'#N/A' ) AS STATS_TRGT_VL -- NULL은 '#N/A'로 대체
FROM GSCN_DIAG_MTST A
INNER JOIN (SELECT DISTINCT HCODE, PTNO, ADD_DAYS(BRTH, 14) AS BRTH, SEX FROM CNCR_RGST WHERE BRTH IS NOT NULL AND POPCODE = '04' ) B -- '04' 위암
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HCODE
AND A.PT_SBST_NO = B.PTNO
AND A.MTDG_YMD BETWEEN '20100101' AND '20211231'
)

FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL) AS A  
INNER JOIN (SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS WHOL_NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  WHOL_PT_CNT

ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=B.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = B.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = B.PT_SEX_CD

B.SEX AS PT_SEX_CD, A.CEXM_SMCT_NM as STATS_TRGT_COL,

ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HCODE
AND A.PT_SBST_NO = B.PTNO
AND A.CEXM_YMD BETWEEN '20100101' AND '20211231'
)

(SMRY_STATS_NO, HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, SMRY_STATS_NM, TBL_ID, COL_ID, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, NCS, WHOL_NCS, PT_CNT, WHOL_PT_CNT, STATS_WORK_YMD, COLL_STRT_YMD, COLL_END_YMD, CRTN_DT) 
WITH W1 AS (
SELECT A.HOSP_CD, A.PT_SBST_NO, SUBSTRING(A.IMEX_YMD,1,4) AS CRIT_YR,  
CASE WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.IMEX_YMD)/365.25) <'20' THEN 10 --20세 미만
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.IMEX_YMD)/365.25) <'30' THEN 20  --20대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.IMEX_YMD)/365.25) <'40' THEN 30  --30대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.IMEX_YMD)/365.25) <'50' THEN 40  --40대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.IMEX_YMD)/365.25) <'60' THEN 50  --50대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.IMEX_YMD)/365.25) <'70' THEN 60  --60대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.IMEX_YMD)/365.25) <'80' THEN 70  --70대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.IMEX_YMD)/365.25)  >='80' THEN 80  --80대 이상
   END AS PT_AGE,
B.SEX AS PT_SEX_CD, A.IMEX_SMCT_CD as STATS_TRGT_COL, 
ifnull(A.IMEX_SMCT_CD,'#N/A' ) AS STATS_TRGT_VL -- NULL은 '#N/A'로 대체
FROM GSCN_EXAM_IMAG A
INNER JOIN (SELECT DISTINCT HCODE, PTNO, ADD_DAYS(BRTH, 14) AS BRTH, SEX FROM CNCR_RGST WHERE BRTH IS NOT NULL AND POPCODE = '04' ) B -- '04' 위암
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HCODE
AND A.PT_SBST_NO = B.PTNO
AND A.IMEX_YMD BETWEEN '20100101' AND '20211231'
) 
SELECT 10073 AS SMRY_STATS_NO, A.HOSP_CD, A.CRIT_YR, '위암 영상검사SNOMEDCT코드별' AS SMRY_STATS_NM, 10080 AS TBL_ID, 1008011 AS COL_ID,
cast(A.PT_AGE as INTEGER) as PT_AGE, A.PT_SEX_CD, A.STATS_TRGT_VL, A.NCS,  B.WHOL_NCS, A.PT_CNT, B.WHOL_PT_CNT, 
TO_CHAR(CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,'YYYYMMDD') AS STATS_WORK_YMD, '20100101' AS COLL_STRT_YMD, '20211231' AS COLL_END_YMD, CURRENT_TIMESTAMP AS CRTN_DT FROM 
(SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL) AS A  
INNER JOIN (SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS WHOL_NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  WHOL_PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) AS B  
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=B.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = B.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = B.PT_SEX_CD  
INNER JOIN (select HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, count(STATS_TRGT_COL) as STATS_TRGT_CNT from w1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) C  
ON A.HOSP_CD = C.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=C.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = C.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = C.PT_SEX_CD where C.STATS_TRGT_CNT <> 0;

TO_CHAR(CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,'YYYYMMDD') AS STATS_WORK_YMD, '20100101' AS COLL_STRT_YMD, '20211231' AS COLL_END_YMD, CURRENT_TIMESTAMP AS CRTN_DT FROM 
(SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL) AS A  
INNER JOIN (SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS WHOL_NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  WHOL_PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) AS B  
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=B.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = B.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = B.PT_SEX_CD  
INNER JOIN (select HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, count(STATS_TRGT_COL) as STATS_TRGT_CNT from w1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) C  
ON A.HOSP_CD = C.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=C.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = C.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = C.PT_SEX_CD where C.STATS_TRGT_CNT <> 0;


-- 10079 //위암 분자병리검사소견별

INSERT INTO CNCR_TBL_SMRY_STATS
(SMRY_STATS_NO, HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, SMRY_STATS_NM, TBL_ID, COL_ID, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, NCS, WHOL_NCS, PT_CNT, WHOL_PT_CNT, STATS_WORK_YMD, COLL_STRT_YMD, COLL_END_YMD, CRTN_DT) 
WITH W1 AS (
SELECT A.HOSP_CD, A.PT_SBST_NO, SUBSTRING(A.MLEM_YMD,1,4) AS CRIT_YR,  
CASE WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.MLEM_YMD)/365.25) <'20' THEN 10 --20세 미만
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.MLEM_YMD)/365.25) <'30' THEN 20  --20대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.MLEM_YMD)/365.25) <'40' THEN 30  --30대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.MLEM_YMD)/365.25) <'50' THEN 40  --40대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.MLEM_YMD)/365.25) <'60' THEN 50  --50대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.MLEM_YMD)/365.25) <'70' THEN 60  --60대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.MLEM_YMD)/365.25) <'80' THEN 70  --70대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.MLEM_YMD)/365.25)  >='80' THEN 80  --80대 이상
   END AS PT_AGE,
B.SEX AS PT_SEX_CD, A.MLEM_OPN_CD as STATS_TRGT_COL, 
ifnull(A.MLEM_OPN_CD,'#N/A' ) AS STATS_TRGT_VL -- NULL은 '#N/A'로 대체
FROM GSCN_EXAM_MLPT A
INNER JOIN (SELECT DISTINCT HCODE, PTNO, ADD_DAYS(BRTH, 14) AS BRTH, SEX FROM CNCR_RGST WHERE BRTH IS NOT NULL AND POPCODE = '04' ) B -- '04' 위암
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HCODE
AND A.PT_SBST_NO = B.PTNO
AND A.MLEM_YMD BETWEEN '20100101' AND '20211231'
)

     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.BPSY_YMD)/365.25) <'40' THEN 30  --30대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.BPSY_YMD)/365.25) <'50' THEN 40  --40대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.BPSY_YMD)/365.25) <'60' THEN 50  --50대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.BPSY_YMD)/365.25) <'70' THEN 60  --60대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.BPSY_YMD)/365.25) <'80' THEN 70  --70대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.BPSY_YMD)/365.25)  >='80' THEN 80  --80대 이상
   END AS PT_AGE,
B.SEX AS PT_SEX_CD, A.HTLG_DFGD_CD as STATS_TRGT_COL, 
ifnull(A.HTLG_DFGD_CD,'#N/A' ) AS STATS_TRGT_VL -- NULL은 '#N/A'로 대체
FROM GSCN_EXAM_BYPS A
INNER JOIN (SELECT DISTINCT HCODE, PTNO, ADD_DAYS(BRTH, 14) AS BRTH, SEX FROM CNCR_RGST WHERE BRTH IS NOT NULL AND POPCODE = '04' ) B -- '04' 위암
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HCODE
AND A.PT_SBST_NO = B.PTNO
AND A.BPSY_YMD BETWEEN '20100101' AND '20211231'
) 
SELECT 10084 AS SMRY_STATS_NO, A.HOSP_CD, A.CRIT_YR, '위암 조직학적분화도별' AS SMRY_STATS_NM, 10110 AS TBL_ID, 1011015 AS COL_ID,
cast(A.PT_AGE as INTEGER) as PT_AGE, A.PT_SEX_CD, A.STATS_TRGT_VL, A.NCS,  B.WHOL_NCS, A.PT_CNT, B.WHOL_PT_CNT, 
TO_CHAR(CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,'YYYYMMDD') AS STATS_WORK_YMD, '20100101' AS COLL_STRT_YMD, '20211231' AS COLL_END_YMD, CURRENT_TIMESTAMP AS CRTN_DT FROM 
(SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL) AS A  
INNER JOIN (SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS WHOL_NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  WHOL_PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) AS B  
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=B.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = B.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = B.PT_SEX_CD  
INNER JOIN (select HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, count(STATS_TRGT_COL) as STATS_TRGT_CNT from w1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) C  
ON A.HOSP_CD = C.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=C.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = C.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = C.PT_SEX_CD where C.STATS_TRGT_CNT <> 0;

INNER JOIN (SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS WHOL_NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  WHOL_PT_CNT

ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=B.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = B.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = B.PT_SEX_CD

     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.STMC_EDEX_YMD)/365.25) <'30' THEN 20  --20대

CASE WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.EUS_EXAM_YMD)/365.25) <'20' THEN 10 --20세 미만
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.EUS_EXAM_YMD)/365.25) <'30' THEN 20  --20대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.EUS_EXAM_YMD)/365.25) <'40' THEN 30  --30대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.EUS_EXAM_YMD)/365.25) <'50' THEN 40  --40대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.EUS_EXAM_YMD)/365.25) <'60' THEN 50  --50대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.EUS_EXAM_YMD)/365.25) <'70' THEN 60  --60대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.EUS_EXAM_YMD)/365.25) <'80' THEN 70  --70대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.EUS_EXAM_YMD)/365.25)  >='80' THEN 80  --80대 이상
   END AS PT_AGE,
B.SEX AS PT_SEX_CD, A.EUS_M_STAG_CD as STATS_TRGT_COL, 
ifnull(A.EUS_M_STAG_CD,'#N/A' ) AS STATS_TRGT_VL -- NULL은 '#N/A'로 대체
FROM GSCN_EXAM_EUS A
INNER JOIN (SELECT DISTINCT HCODE, PTNO, ADD_DAYS(BRTH, 14) AS BRTH, SEX FROM CNCR_RGST WHERE BRTH IS NOT NULL AND POPCODE = '04' ) B -- '04' 위암
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HCODE
AND A.PT_SBST_NO = B.PTNO
AND A.EUS_EXAM_YMD BETWEEN '20100101' AND '20211231'
) 
SELECT 10095 AS SMRY_STATS_NO, A.HOSP_CD, A.CRIT_YR, '위암 EUS_M병기별' AS SMRY_STATS_NM, 10140 AS TBL_ID, 1014009 AS COL_ID,
cast(A.PT_AGE as INTEGER) as PT_AGE, A.PT_SEX_CD, A.STATS_TRGT_VL, A.NCS,  B.WHOL_NCS, A.PT_CNT, B.WHOL_PT_CNT, 
TO_CHAR(CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,'YYYYMMDD') AS STATS_WORK_YMD, '20100101' AS COLL_STRT_YMD, '20211231' AS COLL_END_YMD, CURRENT_TIMESTAMP AS CRTN_DT FROM 
(SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL) AS A  
INNER JOIN (SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS WHOL_NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  WHOL_PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) AS B  
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=B.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = B.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = B.PT_SEX_CD  
INNER JOIN (select HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, count(STATS_TRGT_COL) as STATS_TRGT_CNT from w1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) C  
ON A.HOSP_CD = C.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=C.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = C.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = C.PT_SEX_CD where C.STATS_TRGT_CNT <> 0;

INNER JOIN (SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS WHOL_NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  WHOL_PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) AS B  
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=B.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = B.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = B.PT_SEX_CD  
INNER JOIN (select HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, count(STATS_TRGT_COL) as STATS_TRGT_CNT from w1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) C  
ON A.HOSP_CD = C.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=C.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = C.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = C.PT_SEX_CD where C.STATS_TRGT_CNT <> 0;


-- 10101 //위암 수술SNOMEDCT명별

INSERT INTO CNCR_TBL_SMRY_STATS
(SMRY_STATS_NO, HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, SMRY_STATS_NM, TBL_ID, COL_ID, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, NCS, WHOL_NCS, PT_CNT, WHOL_PT_CNT, STATS_WORK_YMD, COLL_STRT_YMD, COLL_END_YMD, CRTN_DT) 
WITH W1 AS (
SELECT A.HOSP_CD, A.PT_SBST_NO, SUBSTRING(A.OPRT_YMD,1,4) AS CRIT_YR,  
CASE WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.OPRT_YMD)/365.25) <'20' THEN 10 --20세 미만
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.OPRT_YMD)/365.25) <'30' THEN 20  --20대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.OPRT_YMD)/365.25) <'40' THEN 30  --30대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.OPRT_YMD)/365.25) <'50' THEN 40  --40대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.OPRT_YMD)/365.25) <'60' THEN 50  --50대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.OPRT_YMD)/365.25) <'70' THEN 60  --60대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.OPRT_YMD)/365.25) <'80' THEN 70  --70대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.OPRT_YMD)/365.25)  >='80' THEN 80  --80대 이상
   END AS PT_AGE,
B.SEX AS PT_SEX_CD, A.OPRT_SMCT_NM as STATS_TRGT_COL, 
ifnull(A.OPRT_SMCT_NM,'#N/A' ) AS STATS_TRGT_VL -- NULL은 '#N/A'로 대체
FROM GSCN_TRTM_OPRT A
INNER JOIN (SELECT DISTINCT HCODE, PTNO, ADD_DAYS(BRTH, 14) AS BRTH, SEX FROM CNCR_RGST WHERE BRTH IS NOT NULL AND POPCODE = '04' ) B -- '04' 위암
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HCODE
AND A.PT_SBST_NO = B.PTNO
AND A.OPRT_YMD BETWEEN '20100101' AND '20211231'
) 
SELECT 10101 AS SMRY_STATS_NO, A.HOSP_CD, A.CRIT_YR, '위암 수술SNOMEDCT명별' AS SMRY_STATS_NM, 10150 AS TBL_ID, 1015012 AS COL_ID,
cast(A.PT_AGE as INTEGER) as PT_AGE, A.PT_SEX_CD, A.STATS_TRGT_VL, A.NCS,  B.WHOL_NCS, A.PT_CNT, B.WHOL_PT_CNT, 
TO_CHAR(CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,'YYYYMMDD') AS STATS_WORK_YMD, '20100101' AS COLL_STRT_YMD, '20211231' AS COLL_END_YMD, CURRENT_TIMESTAMP AS CRTN_DT FROM 
(SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL) AS A  
INNER JOIN (SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS WHOL_NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  WHOL_PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) AS B  
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=B.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = B.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = B.PT_SEX_CD  
INNER JOIN (select HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, count(STATS_TRGT_COL) as STATS_TRGT_CNT from w1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) C  
ON A.HOSP_CD = C.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=C.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = C.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = C.PT_SEX_CD where C.STATS_TRGT_CNT <> 0;

ifnull(A.ASA_SCOR_CD,'#N/A' ) AS STATS_TRGT_VL -- NULL은 '#N/A'로 대체
FROM GSCN_TRTM_OPRT A
INNER JOIN (SELECT DISTINCT HCODE, PTNO, ADD_DAYS(BRTH, 14) AS BRTH, SEX FROM CNCR_RGST WHERE BRTH IS NOT NULL AND POPCODE = '04' ) B -- '04' 위암
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HCODE
AND A.PT_SBST_NO = B.PTNO
AND A.OPRT_YMD BETWEEN '20100101' AND '20211231'
) 
SELECT 10106 AS SMRY_STATS_NO, A.HOSP_CD, A.CRIT_YR, '위암 ASA점수별' AS SMRY_STATS_NM, 10150 AS TBL_ID, 1015022 AS COL_ID,
cast(A.PT_AGE as INTEGER) as PT_AGE, A.PT_SEX_CD, A.STATS_TRGT_VL, A.NCS,  B.WHOL_NCS, A.PT_CNT, B.WHOL_PT_CNT, 
TO_CHAR(CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,'YYYYMMDD') AS STATS_WORK_YMD, '20100101' AS COLL_STRT_YMD, '20211231' AS COLL_END_YMD, CURRENT_TIMESTAMP AS CRTN_DT FROM

INNER JOIN (SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS WHOL_NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  WHOL_PT_CNT

ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=B.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = B.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = B.PT_SEX_CD

ON A.HOSP_CD = C.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=C.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = C.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = C.PT_SEX_CD where C.STATS_TRGT_CNT <> 0;


-- 10112 //위암 수술장내시경사용여부확인불가구분별

INSERT INTO CNCR_TBL_SMRY_STATS
(SMRY_STATS_NO, HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, SMRY_STATS_NM, TBL_ID, COL_ID, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, NCS, WHOL_NCS, PT_CNT, WHOL_PT_CNT, STATS_WORK_YMD, COLL_STRT_YMD, COLL_END_YMD, CRTN_DT) 
WITH W1 AS (
SELECT A.HOSP_CD, A.PT_SBST_NO, SUBSTRING(A.OPRT_YMD,1,4) AS CRIT_YR,  
CASE WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.OPRT_YMD)/365.25) <'20' THEN 10 --20세 미만
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.OPRT_YMD)/365.25) <'30' THEN 20  --20대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.OPRT_YMD)/365.25) <'40' THEN 30  --30대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.OPRT_YMD)/365.25) <'50' THEN 40  --40대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.OPRT_YMD)/365.25) <'60' THEN 50  --50대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.OPRT_YMD)/365.25) <'70' THEN 60  --60대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.OPRT_YMD)/365.25) <'80' THEN 70  --70대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.OPRT_YMD)/365.25)  >='80' THEN 80  --80대 이상
   END AS PT_AGE,
B.SEX AS PT_SEX_CD, A.OPRM_ENSP_USE_YN_UNID_SPCD as STATS_TRGT_COL, 
ifnull(A.OPRM_ENSP_USE_YN_UNID_SPCD,'#N/A' ) AS STATS_TRGT_VL -- NULL은 '#N/A'로 대체
FROM GSCN_TRTM_OPRT A
INNER JOIN (SELECT DISTINCT HCODE, PTNO, ADD_DAYS(BRTH, 14) AS BRTH, SEX FROM CNCR_RGST WHERE BRTH IS NOT NULL AND POPCODE = '04' ) B -- '04' 위암
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HCODE
AND A.PT_SBST_NO = B.PTNO
AND A.OPRT_YMD BETWEEN '20100101' AND '20211231'
) 
SELECT 10112 AS SMRY_STATS_NO, A.HOSP_CD, A.CRIT_YR, '위암 수술장내시경사용여부확인불가구분별' AS SMRY_STATS_NM, 10150 AS TBL_ID, 1015034 AS COL_ID,
cast(A.PT_AGE as INTEGER) as PT_AGE, A.PT_SEX_CD, A.STATS_TRGT_VL, A.NCS,  B.WHOL_NCS, A.PT_CNT, B.WHOL_PT_CNT, 
TO_CHAR(CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,'YYYYMMDD') AS STATS_WORK_YMD, '20100101' AS COLL_STRT_YMD, '20211231' AS COLL_END_YMD, CURRENT_TIMESTAMP AS CRTN_DT FROM 
(SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL) AS A  
INNER JOIN (SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS WHOL_NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  WHOL_PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) AS B  
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=B.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = B.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = B.PT_SEX_CD  
INNER JOIN (select HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, count(STATS_TRGT_COL) as STATS_TRGT_CNT from w1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) C  
ON A.HOSP_CD = C.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=C.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = C.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = C.PT_SEX_CD where C.STATS_TRGT_CNT <> 0;

ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HCODE
AND A.PT_SBST_NO = B.PTNO
AND A.OPRT_YMD BETWEEN '20100101' AND '20211231'
)

(SMRY_STATS_NO, HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, SMRY_STATS_NM, TBL_ID, COL_ID, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, NCS, WHOL_NCS, PT_CNT, WHOL_PT_CNT, STATS_WORK_YMD, COLL_STRT_YMD, COLL_END_YMD, CRTN_DT) 
WITH W1 AS (
SELECT A.HOSP_CD, A.PT_SBST_NO, SUBSTRING(A.OPRT_YMD,1,4) AS CRIT_YR,  
CASE WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.OPRT_YMD)/365.25) <'20' THEN 10 --20세 미만
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.OPRT_YMD)/365.25) <'30' THEN 20  --20대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.OPRT_YMD)/365.25) <'40' THEN 30  --30대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.OPRT_YMD)/365.25) <'50' THEN 40  --40대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.OPRT_YMD)/365.25) <'60' THEN 50  --50대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.OPRT_YMD)/365.25) <'70' THEN 60  --60대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.OPRT_YMD)/365.25) <'80' THEN 70  --70대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.OPRT_YMD)/365.25)  >='80' THEN 80  --80대 이상
   END AS PT_AGE,
B.SEX AS PT_SEX_CD, A.REPR_USE_DVCE_NM as STATS_TRGT_COL, 
ifnull(A.REPR_USE_DVCE_NM,'#N/A' ) AS STATS_TRGT_VL -- NULL은 '#N/A'로 대체
FROM GSCN_TRTM_OPRT A
INNER JOIN (SELECT DISTINCT HCODE, PTNO, ADD_DAYS(BRTH, 14) AS BRTH, SEX FROM CNCR_RGST WHERE BRTH IS NOT NULL AND POPCODE = '04' ) B -- '04' 위암
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HCODE
AND A.PT_SBST_NO = B.PTNO
AND A.OPRT_YMD BETWEEN '20100101' AND '20211231'
) 
SELECT 10123 AS SMRY_STATS_NO, A.HOSP_CD, A.CRIT_YR, '위암 재건술사용도구명별' AS SMRY_STATS_NM, 10150 AS TBL_ID, 1015054 AS COL_ID,
cast(A.PT_AGE as INTEGER) as PT_AGE, A.PT_SEX_CD, A.STATS_TRGT_VL, A.NCS,  B.WHOL_NCS, A.PT_CNT, B.WHOL_PT_CNT, 
TO_CHAR(CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,'YYYYMMDD') AS STATS_WORK_YMD, '20100101' AS COLL_STRT_YMD, '20211231' AS COLL_END_YMD, CURRENT_TIMESTAMP AS CRTN_DT FROM 
(SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL) AS A  
INNER JOIN (SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS WHOL_NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  WHOL_PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) AS B  
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=B.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = B.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = B.PT_SEX_CD  
INNER JOIN (select HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, count(STATS_TRGT_COL) as STATS_TRGT_CNT from w1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) C  
ON A.HOSP_CD = C.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=C.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = C.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = C.PT_SEX_CD where C.STATS_TRGT_CNT <> 0;

(SMRY_STATS_NO, HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, SMRY_STATS_NM, TBL_ID, COL_ID, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, NCS, WHOL_NCS, PT_CNT, WHOL_PT_CNT, STATS_WORK_YMD, COLL_STRT_YMD, COLL_END_YMD, CRTN_DT) 
WITH W1 AS (
SELECT A.HOSP_CD, A.PT_SBST_NO, SUBSTRING(A.ESD_SRPR_YMD,1,4) AS CRIT_YR,  
CASE WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ESD_SRPR_YMD)/365.25) <'20' THEN 10 --20세 미만
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ESD_SRPR_YMD)/365.25) <'30' THEN 20  --20대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ESD_SRPR_YMD)/365.25) <'40' THEN 30  --30대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ESD_SRPR_YMD)/365.25) <'50' THEN 40  --40대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ESD_SRPR_YMD)/365.25) <'60' THEN 50  --50대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ESD_SRPR_YMD)/365.25) <'70' THEN 60  --60대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ESD_SRPR_YMD)/365.25) <'80' THEN 70  --70대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ESD_SRPR_YMD)/365.25)  >='80' THEN 80  --80대 이상
   END AS PT_AGE,
B.SEX AS PT_SEX_CD, A.ESD_LESN_SHAP_CD as STATS_TRGT_COL, 
ifnull(A.ESD_LESN_SHAP_CD,'#N/A' ) AS STATS_TRGT_VL -- NULL은 '#N/A'로 대체
FROM GSCN_TRTM_SRPR A
INNER JOIN (SELECT DISTINCT HCODE, PTNO, ADD_DAYS(BRTH, 14) AS BRTH, SEX FROM CNCR_RGST WHERE BRTH IS NOT NULL AND POPCODE = '04' ) B -- '04' 위암
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HCODE
AND A.PT_SBST_NO = B.PTNO
AND A.ESD_SRPR_YMD BETWEEN '20100101' AND '20211231'
)

(SMRY_STATS_NO, HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, SMRY_STATS_NM, TBL_ID, COL_ID, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, NCS, WHOL_NCS, PT_CNT, WHOL_PT_CNT, STATS_WORK_YMD, COLL_STRT_YMD, COLL_END_YMD, CRTN_DT) 
WITH W1 AS (
SELECT A.HOSP_CD, A.PT_SBST_NO, SUBSTRING(A.ESD_SRPR_YMD,1,4) AS CRIT_YR,  
CASE WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ESD_SRPR_YMD)/365.25) <'20' THEN 10 --20세 미만
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ESD_SRPR_YMD)/365.25) <'30' THEN 20  --20대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ESD_SRPR_YMD)/365.25) <'40' THEN 30  --30대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ESD_SRPR_YMD)/365.25) <'50' THEN 40  --40대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ESD_SRPR_YMD)/365.25) <'60' THEN 50  --50대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ESD_SRPR_YMD)/365.25) <'70' THEN 60  --60대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ESD_SRPR_YMD)/365.25) <'80' THEN 70  --70대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ESD_SRPR_YMD)/365.25)  >='80' THEN 80  --80대 이상
   END AS PT_AGE,
B.SEX AS PT_SEX_CD, A.ESD_PERF_MSRE_CD as STATS_TRGT_COL, 
ifnull(A.ESD_PERF_MSRE_CD,'#N/A' ) AS STATS_TRGT_VL -- NULL은 '#N/A'로 대체
FROM GSCN_TRTM_SRPR A
INNER JOIN (SELECT DISTINCT HCODE, PTNO, ADD_DAYS(BRTH, 14) AS BRTH, SEX FROM CNCR_RGST WHERE BRTH IS NOT NULL AND POPCODE = '04' ) B -- '04' 위암
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HCODE
AND A.PT_SBST_NO = B.PTNO
AND A.ESD_SRPR_YMD BETWEEN '20100101' AND '20211231'
) 
SELECT 10134 AS SMRY_STATS_NO, A.HOSP_CD, A.CRIT_YR, '위암 ESD천공조치별' AS SMRY_STATS_NM, 10160 AS TBL_ID, 1016018 AS COL_ID,
cast(A.PT_AGE as INTEGER) as PT_AGE, A.PT_SEX_CD, A.STATS_TRGT_VL, A.NCS,  B.WHOL_NCS, A.PT_CNT, B.WHOL_PT_CNT, 
TO_CHAR(CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,'YYYYMMDD') AS STATS_WORK_YMD, '20100101' AS COLL_STRT_YMD, '20211231' AS COLL_END_YMD, CURRENT_TIMESTAMP AS CRTN_DT FROM 
(SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL) AS A  
INNER JOIN (SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS WHOL_NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  WHOL_PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) AS B  
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=B.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = B.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = B.PT_SEX_CD  
INNER JOIN (select HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, count(STATS_TRGT_COL) as STATS_TRGT_CNT from w1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) C  
ON A.HOSP_CD = C.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=C.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = C.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = C.PT_SEX_CD where C.STATS_TRGT_CNT <> 0;

AND A.SRGC_PTEM_YMD BETWEEN '20100101' AND '20211231'
)

     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.SRGC_PTEM_YMD)/365.25) <'30' THEN 20  --20대

-- 10145 //위암 종양가로길이별

(SMRY_STATS_NO, HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, SMRY_STATS_NM, TBL_ID, COL_ID, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, NCS, WHOL_NCS, PT_CNT, WHOL_PT_CNT, STATS_WORK_YMD, COLL_STRT_YMD, COLL_END_YMD, CRTN_DT) 
WITH W1 AS (
SELECT A.HOSP_CD, A.PT_SBST_NO, SUBSTRING(A.SRGC_PTEM_YMD,1,4) AS CRIT_YR, 
CASE WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.SRGC_PTEM_YMD)/365.25) <'20' THEN 10 --20세 미만
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.SRGC_PTEM_YMD)/365.25) <'30' THEN 20  --20대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.SRGC_PTEM_YMD)/365.25) <'40' THEN 30  --30대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.SRGC_PTEM_YMD)/365.25) <'50' THEN 40  --40대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.SRGC_PTEM_YMD)/365.25) <'60' THEN 50  --50대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.SRGC_PTEM_YMD)/365.25) <'70' THEN 60  --60대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.SRGC_PTEM_YMD)/365.25) <'80' THEN 70  --70대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.SRGC_PTEM_YMD)/365.25)  >='80' THEN 80  --80대 이상
   END AS PT_AGE,
B.SEX AS PT_SEX_CD, A.TUMR_WDTH_LNTH_VL as STATS_TRGT_COL, 
ifnull(TO_CHAR(A.TUMR_WDTH_LNTH_VL),'#N/A' ) AS STATS_TRGT_VL -- NUMERIC 컬럼 변환(NULL은 '#N/A'로 대체)
FROM GSCN_EXAM_SGPT A
INNER JOIN (SELECT DISTINCT HCODE, PTNO, ADD_DAYS(BRTH, 14) AS BRTH, SEX FROM CNCR_RGST WHERE BRTH IS NOT NULL AND POPCODE = '04' ) B -- '04'위암
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HCODE
AND A.PT_SBST_NO = B.PTNO
AND A.SRGC_PTEM_YMD BETWEEN '20100101' AND '20211231'
) 
SELECT 10145 AS SMRY_STATS_NO, A.HOSP_CD, A.CRIT_YR, '위암 종양가로길이별' AS SMRY_STATS_NM, 10170 AS TBL_ID, 1017022 AS COL_ID,
cast(A.PT_AGE as INTEGER) as PT_AGE, A.PT_SEX_CD, A.STATS_TRGT_VL, A.NCS,  B.WHOL_NCS, A.PT_CNT, B.WHOL_PT_CNT, 
TO_CHAR(CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,'YYYYMMDD') AS STATS_WORK_YMD, '20100101' AS COLL_STRT_YMD, '20211231' AS COLL_END_YMD, CURRENT_TIMESTAMP AS CRTN_DT FROM 
(SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL) AS A  
INNER JOIN (SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS WHOL_NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  WHOL_PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) AS B  
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=B.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = B.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = B.PT_SEX_CD  
INNER JOIN (select HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, count(STATS_TRGT_COL) as STATS_TRGT_CNT from w1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) C  
ON A.HOSP_CD = C.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=C.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = C.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = C.PT_SEX_CD where C.STATS_TRGT_CNT <> 0;

AND A.SRGC_PTEM_YMD BETWEEN '20100101' AND '20211231'
) 
SELECT 10150 AS SMRY_STATS_NO, A.HOSP_CD, A.CRIT_YR, '위암 침윤정도별' AS SMRY_STATS_NM, 10170 AS TBL_ID, 1017028 AS COL_ID,
cast(A.PT_AGE as INTEGER) as PT_AGE, A.PT_SEX_CD, A.STATS_TRGT_VL, A.NCS,  B.WHOL_NCS, A.PT_CNT, B.WHOL_PT_CNT, 
TO_CHAR(CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,'YYYYMMDD') AS STATS_WORK_YMD, '20100101' AS COLL_STRT_YMD, '20211231' AS COLL_END_YMD, CURRENT_TIMESTAMP AS CRTN_DT FROM 
(SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL) AS A  
INNER JOIN (SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS WHOL_NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  WHOL_PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) AS B  
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=B.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = B.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = B.PT_SEX_CD  
INNER JOIN (select HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, count(STATS_TRGT_COL) as STATS_TRGT_CNT from w1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) C  
ON A.HOSP_CD = C.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=C.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = C.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = C.PT_SEX_CD where C.STATS_TRGT_CNT <> 0;


-- 10151 //위암 침윤깊이별

INSERT INTO CNCR_TBL_SMRY_STATS
(SMRY_STATS_NO, HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, SMRY_STATS_NM, TBL_ID, COL_ID, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, NCS, WHOL_NCS, PT_CNT, WHOL_PT_CNT, STATS_WORK_YMD, COLL_STRT_YMD, COLL_END_YMD, CRTN_DT) 
WITH W1 AS (
SELECT A.HOSP_CD, A.PT_SBST_NO, SUBSTRING(A.SRGC_PTEM_YMD,1,4) AS CRIT_YR, 
CASE WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.SRGC_PTEM_YMD)/365.25) <'20' THEN 10 --20세 미만
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.SRGC_PTEM_YMD)/365.25) <'30' THEN 20  --20대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.SRGC_PTEM_YMD)/365.25) <'40' THEN 30  --30대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.SRGC_PTEM_YMD)/365.25) <'50' THEN 40  --40대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.SRGC_PTEM_YMD)/365.25) <'60' THEN 50  --50대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.SRGC_PTEM_YMD)/365.25) <'70' THEN 60  --60대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.SRGC_PTEM_YMD)/365.25) <'80' THEN 70  --70대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.SRGC_PTEM_YMD)/365.25)  >='80' THEN 80  --80대 이상
   END AS PT_AGE,
B.SEX AS PT_SEX_CD, A.INVA_DPTH_VL as STATS_TRGT_COL, 
ifnull(TO_CHAR(A.INVA_DPTH_VL),'#N/A' ) AS STATS_TRGT_VL -- NUMERIC 컬럼 변환(NULL은 '#N/A'로 대체)
FROM GSCN_EXAM_SGPT A
INNER JOIN (SELECT DISTINCT HCODE, PTNO, ADD_DAYS(BRTH, 14) AS BRTH, SEX FROM CNCR_RGST WHERE BRTH IS NOT NULL AND POPCODE = '04' ) B -- '04'위암
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HCODE
AND A.PT_SBST_NO = B.PTNO
AND A.SRGC_PTEM_YMD BETWEEN '20100101' AND '20211231'
) 
SELECT 10151 AS SMRY_STATS_NO, A.HOSP_CD, A.CRIT_YR, '위암 침윤깊이별' AS SMRY_STATS_NM, 10170 AS TBL_ID, 1017030 AS COL_ID,
cast(A.PT_AGE as INTEGER) as PT_AGE, A.PT_SEX_CD, A.STATS_TRGT_VL, A.NCS,  B.WHOL_NCS, A.PT_CNT, B.WHOL_PT_CNT, 
TO_CHAR(CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,'YYYYMMDD') AS STATS_WORK_YMD, '20100101' AS COLL_STRT_YMD, '20211231' AS COLL_END_YMD, CURRENT_TIMESTAMP AS CRTN_DT FROM 
(SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL) AS A  
INNER JOIN (SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS WHOL_NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  WHOL_PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) AS B  
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=B.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = B.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = B.PT_SEX_CD  
INNER JOIN (select HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, count(STATS_TRGT_COL) as STATS_TRGT_CNT from w1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) C  
ON A.HOSP_CD = C.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=C.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = C.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = C.PT_SEX_CD where C.STATS_TRGT_CNT <> 0;

-- 10156 //위암 수술근위절제면크기별

INSERT INTO CNCR_TBL_SMRY_STATS
(SMRY_STATS_NO, HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, SMRY_STATS_NM, TBL_ID, COL_ID, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, NCS, WHOL_NCS, PT_CNT, WHOL_PT_CNT, STATS_WORK_YMD, COLL_STRT_YMD, COLL_END_YMD, CRTN_DT) 
WITH W1 AS (
SELECT A.HOSP_CD, A.PT_SBST_NO, SUBSTRING(A.SRGC_PTEM_YMD,1,4) AS CRIT_YR, 
CASE WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.SRGC_PTEM_YMD)/365.25) <'20' THEN 10 --20세 미만
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.SRGC_PTEM_YMD)/365.25) <'30' THEN 20  --20대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.SRGC_PTEM_YMD)/365.25) <'40' THEN 30  --30대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.SRGC_PTEM_YMD)/365.25) <'50' THEN 40  --40대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.SRGC_PTEM_YMD)/365.25) <'60' THEN 50  --50대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.SRGC_PTEM_YMD)/365.25) <'70' THEN 60  --60대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.SRGC_PTEM_YMD)/365.25) <'80' THEN 70  --70대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.SRGC_PTEM_YMD)/365.25)  >='80' THEN 80  --80대 이상
   END AS PT_AGE,
B.SEX AS PT_SEX_CD, A.OPRT_PMRG_SIZE_VL as STATS_TRGT_COL, 
ifnull(TO_CHAR(A.OPRT_PMRG_SIZE_VL),'#N/A' ) AS STATS_TRGT_VL -- NUMERIC 컬럼 변환(NULL은 '#N/A'로 대체)
FROM GSCN_EXAM_SGPT A
INNER JOIN (SELECT DISTINCT HCODE, PTNO, ADD_DAYS(BRTH, 14) AS BRTH, SEX FROM CNCR_RGST WHERE BRTH IS NOT NULL AND POPCODE = '04' ) B -- '04'위암
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HCODE
AND A.PT_SBST_NO = B.PTNO
AND A.SRGC_PTEM_YMD BETWEEN '20100101' AND '20211231'
) 
SELECT 10156 AS SMRY_STATS_NO, A.HOSP_CD, A.CRIT_YR, '위암 수술근위절제면크기별' AS SMRY_STATS_NM, 10170 AS TBL_ID, 1017039 AS COL_ID,
cast(A.PT_AGE as INTEGER) as PT_AGE, A.PT_SEX_CD, A.STATS_TRGT_VL, A.NCS,  B.WHOL_NCS, A.PT_CNT, B.WHOL_PT_CNT, 
TO_CHAR(CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,'YYYYMMDD') AS STATS_WORK_YMD, '20100101' AS COLL_STRT_YMD, '20211231' AS COLL_END_YMD, CURRENT_TIMESTAMP AS CRTN_DT FROM 
(SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL) AS A  
INNER JOIN (SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS WHOL_NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  WHOL_PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) AS B  
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=B.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = B.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = B.PT_SEX_CD  
INNER JOIN (select HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, count(STATS_TRGT_COL) as STATS_TRGT_CNT from w1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) C  
ON A.HOSP_CD = C.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=C.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = C.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = C.PT_SEX_CD where C.STATS_TRGT_CNT <> 0;

B.SEX AS PT_SEX_CD, A.PSTV_LN_CNT as STATS_TRGT_COL, 
ifnull(A.PSTV_LN_CNT,'#N/A' ) AS STATS_TRGT_VL -- NULL은 '#N/A'로 대체
FROM GSCN_EXAM_SGPT A
INNER JOIN (SELECT DISTINCT HCODE, PTNO, ADD_DAYS(BRTH, 14) AS BRTH, SEX FROM CNCR_RGST WHERE BRTH IS NOT NULL AND POPCODE = '04' ) B -- '04' 위암
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HCODE
AND A.PT_SBST_NO = B.PTNO
AND A.SRGC_PTEM_YMD BETWEEN '20100101' AND '20211231'
) 
SELECT 10161 AS SMRY_STATS_NO, A.HOSP_CD, A.CRIT_YR, '위암 양성림프절수별' AS SMRY_STATS_NM, 10170 AS TBL_ID, 1017046 AS COL_ID,
cast(A.PT_AGE as INTEGER) as PT_AGE, A.PT_SEX_CD, A.STATS_TRGT_VL, A.NCS,  B.WHOL_NCS, A.PT_CNT, B.WHOL_PT_CNT, 
TO_CHAR(CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,'YYYYMMDD') AS STATS_WORK_YMD, '20100101' AS COLL_STRT_YMD, '20211231' AS COLL_END_YMD, CURRENT_TIMESTAMP AS CRTN_DT FROM 
(SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL) AS A  
INNER JOIN (SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS WHOL_NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  WHOL_PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) AS B  
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=B.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = B.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = B.PT_SEX_CD

INNER JOIN (select HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, count(STATS_TRGT_COL) as STATS_TRGT_CNT from w1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) C  
ON A.HOSP_CD = C.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=C.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = C.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = C.PT_SEX_CD where C.STATS_TRGT_CNT <> 0;


-- 10167 //위암 ESD수직절제면잔존암양성여부별

INSERT INTO CNCR_TBL_SMRY_STATS
(SMRY_STATS_NO, HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, SMRY_STATS_NM, TBL_ID, COL_ID, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, NCS, WHOL_NCS, PT_CNT, WHOL_PT_CNT, STATS_WORK_YMD, COLL_STRT_YMD, COLL_END_YMD, CRTN_DT) 
WITH W1 AS (
SELECT A.HOSP_CD, A.PT_SBST_NO, SUBSTRING(A.SRGC_PTEM_YMD,1,4) AS CRIT_YR,  
CASE WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.SRGC_PTEM_YMD)/365.25) <'20' THEN 10 --20세 미만
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.SRGC_PTEM_YMD)/365.25) <'30' THEN 20  --20대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.SRGC_PTEM_YMD)/365.25) <'40' THEN 30  --30대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.SRGC_PTEM_YMD)/365.25) <'50' THEN 40  --40대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.SRGC_PTEM_YMD)/365.25) <'60' THEN 50  --50대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.SRGC_PTEM_YMD)/365.25) <'70' THEN 60  --60대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.SRGC_PTEM_YMD)/365.25) <'80' THEN 70  --70대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.SRGC_PTEM_YMD)/365.25)  >='80' THEN 80  --80대 이상
   END AS PT_AGE,
B.SEX AS PT_SEX_CD, A.ESD_VMRG_RLCR_PSTV_YN_SPCD as STATS_TRGT_COL, 
ifnull(A.ESD_VMRG_RLCR_PSTV_YN_SPCD,'#N/A' ) AS STATS_TRGT_VL -- NULL은 '#N/A'로 대체
FROM GSCN_EXAM_SGPT A
INNER JOIN (SELECT DISTINCT HCODE, PTNO, ADD_DAYS(BRTH, 14) AS BRTH, SEX FROM CNCR_RGST WHERE BRTH IS NOT NULL AND POPCODE = '04' ) B -- '04' 위암
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HCODE
AND A.PT_SBST_NO = B.PTNO
AND A.SRGC_PTEM_YMD BETWEEN '20100101' AND '20211231'
) 
SELECT 10167 AS SMRY_STATS_NO, A.HOSP_CD, A.CRIT_YR, '위암 ESD수직절제면잔존암양성여부별' AS SMRY_STATS_NM, 10170 AS TBL_ID, 1017053 AS COL_ID,
cast(A.PT_AGE as INTEGER) as PT_AGE, A.PT_SEX_CD, A.STATS_TRGT_VL, A.NCS,  B.WHOL_NCS, A.PT_CNT, B.WHOL_PT_CNT, 
TO_CHAR(CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,'YYYYMMDD') AS STATS_WORK_YMD, '20100101' AS COLL_STRT_YMD, '20211231' AS COLL_END_YMD, CURRENT_TIMESTAMP AS CRTN_DT FROM 
(SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL) AS A  
INNER JOIN (SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS WHOL_NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  WHOL_PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) AS B  
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=B.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = B.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = B.PT_SEX_CD  
INNER JOIN (select HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, count(STATS_TRGT_COL) as STATS_TRGT_CNT from w1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) C

     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.COMP_OCRN_OPRT_YMD)/365.25) <'60' THEN 50  --50대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.COMP_OCRN_OPRT_YMD)/365.25) <'70' THEN 60  --60대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.COMP_OCRN_OPRT_YMD)/365.25) <'80' THEN 70  --70대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.COMP_OCRN_OPRT_YMD)/365.25)  >='80' THEN 80  --80대 이상
   END AS PT_AGE,
B.SEX AS PT_SEX_CD, A.AFOC_CLCD as STATS_TRGT_COL, 
ifnull(A.AFOC_CLCD,'#N/A' ) AS STATS_TRGT_VL -- NULL은 '#N/A'로 대체
FROM GSCN_DIAG_AFOC A
INNER JOIN (SELECT DISTINCT HCODE, PTNO, ADD_DAYS(BRTH, 14) AS BRTH, SEX FROM CNCR_RGST WHERE BRTH IS NOT NULL AND POPCODE = '04' ) B -- '04' 위암
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HCODE
AND A.PT_SBST_NO = B.PTNO
AND A.COMP_OCRN_OPRT_YMD BETWEEN '20100101' AND '20211231'
) 
SELECT 10172 AS SMRY_STATS_NO, A.HOSP_CD, A.CRIT_YR, '위암 수술후합병증분류별' AS SMRY_STATS_NM, 10180 AS TBL_ID, 1018005 AS COL_ID,
cast(A.PT_AGE as INTEGER) as PT_AGE, A.PT_SEX_CD, A.STATS_TRGT_VL, A.NCS,  B.WHOL_NCS, A.PT_CNT, B.WHOL_PT_CNT, 
TO_CHAR(CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,'YYYYMMDD') AS STATS_WORK_YMD, '20100101' AS COLL_STRT_YMD, '20211231' AS COLL_END_YMD, CURRENT_TIMESTAMP AS CRTN_DT FROM 
(SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL) AS A  
INNER JOIN (SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS WHOL_NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  WHOL_PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) AS B  
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=B.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = B.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = B.PT_SEX_CD  
INNER JOIN (select HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, count(STATS_TRGT_COL) as STATS_TRGT_CNT from w1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) C  
ON A.HOSP_CD = C.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=C.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = C.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = C.PT_SEX_CD where C.STATS_TRGT_CNT <> 0;

FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL) AS A  
INNER JOIN (SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS WHOL_NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  WHOL_PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) AS B  
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=B.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = B.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = B.PT_SEX_CD  
INNER JOIN (select HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, count(STATS_TRGT_COL) as STATS_TRGT_CNT from w1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) C  
ON A.HOSP_CD = C.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=C.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = C.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = C.PT_SEX_CD where C.STATS_TRGT_CNT <> 0;


-- 10178 //위암 약제구분별

INSERT INTO CNCR_TBL_SMRY_STATS
(SMRY_STATS_NO, HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, SMRY_STATS_NM, TBL_ID, COL_ID, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, NCS, WHOL_NCS, PT_CNT, WHOL_PT_CNT, STATS_WORK_YMD, COLL_STRT_YMD, COLL_END_YMD, CRTN_DT) 
WITH W1 AS (
SELECT A.HOSP_CD, A.PT_SBST_NO, SUBSTRING(A.DRUG_PRSC_YMD,1,4) AS CRIT_YR,  
CASE WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.DRUG_PRSC_YMD)/365.25) <'20' THEN 10 --20세 미만
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.DRUG_PRSC_YMD)/365.25) <'30' THEN 20  --20대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.DRUG_PRSC_YMD)/365.25) <'40' THEN 30  --30대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.DRUG_PRSC_YMD)/365.25) <'50' THEN 40  --40대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.DRUG_PRSC_YMD)/365.25) <'60' THEN 50  --50대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.DRUG_PRSC_YMD)/365.25) <'70' THEN 60  --60대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.DRUG_PRSC_YMD)/365.25) <'80' THEN 70  --70대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.DRUG_PRSC_YMD)/365.25)  >='80' THEN 80  --80대 이상
   END AS PT_AGE,
B.SEX AS PT_SEX_CD, A.DRUG_SPCD as STATS_TRGT_COL, 
ifnull(A.DRUG_SPCD,'#N/A' ) AS STATS_TRGT_VL -- NULL은 '#N/A'로 대체
FROM GSCN_TRTM_DRIN A
INNER JOIN (SELECT DISTINCT HCODE, PTNO, ADD_DAYS(BRTH, 14) AS BRTH, SEX FROM CNCR_RGST WHERE BRTH IS NOT NULL AND POPCODE = '04' ) B -- '04' 위암
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HCODE
AND A.PT_SBST_NO = B.PTNO
AND A.DRUG_PRSC_YMD BETWEEN '20100101' AND '20211231'
) 
SELECT 10178 AS SMRY_STATS_NO, A.HOSP_CD, A.CRIT_YR, '위암 약제구분별' AS SMRY_STATS_NM, 10200 AS TBL_ID, 1020007 AS COL_ID,
cast(A.PT_AGE as INTEGER) as PT_AGE, A.PT_SEX_CD, A.STATS_TRGT_VL, A.NCS,  B.WHOL_NCS, A.PT_CNT, B.WHOL_PT_CNT, 
TO_CHAR(CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,'YYYYMMDD') AS STATS_WORK_YMD, '20100101' AS COLL_STRT_YMD, '20211231' AS COLL_END_YMD, CURRENT_TIMESTAMP AS CRTN_DT FROM 
(SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL) AS A  
INNER JOIN (SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS WHOL_NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  WHOL_PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) AS B  
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=B.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = B.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = B.PT_SEX_CD  
INNER JOIN (select HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, count(STATS_TRGT_COL) as STATS_TRGT_CNT from w1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) C

     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.DRUG_PRSC_YMD)/365.25) <'60' THEN 50  --50대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.DRUG_PRSC_YMD)/365.25) <'70' THEN 60  --60대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.DRUG_PRSC_YMD)/365.25) <'80' THEN 70  --70대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.DRUG_PRSC_YMD)/365.25)  >='80' THEN 80  --80대 이상
   END AS PT_AGE,
B.SEX AS PT_SEX_CD, A.DRIN_SMCT_NM as STATS_TRGT_COL, 
ifnull(A.DRIN_SMCT_NM,'#N/A' ) AS STATS_TRGT_VL -- NULL은 '#N/A'로 대체
FROM GSCN_TRTM_DRIN A
INNER JOIN (SELECT DISTINCT HCODE, PTNO, ADD_DAYS(BRTH, 14) AS BRTH, SEX FROM CNCR_RGST WHERE BRTH IS NOT NULL AND POPCODE = '04' ) B -- '04' 위암
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HCODE
AND A.PT_SBST_NO = B.PTNO
AND A.DRUG_PRSC_YMD BETWEEN '20100101' AND '20211231'
) 
SELECT 10183 AS SMRY_STATS_NO, A.HOSP_CD, A.CRIT_YR, '위암 약제성분SNOMEDCT명별' AS SMRY_STATS_NM, 10200 AS TBL_ID, 1020014 AS COL_ID,
cast(A.PT_AGE as INTEGER) as PT_AGE, A.PT_SEX_CD, A.STATS_TRGT_VL, A.NCS,  B.WHOL_NCS, A.PT_CNT, B.WHOL_PT_CNT, 
TO_CHAR(CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,'YYYYMMDD') AS STATS_WORK_YMD, '20100101' AS COLL_STRT_YMD, '20211231' AS COLL_END_YMD, CURRENT_TIMESTAMP AS CRTN_DT FROM 
(SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL) AS A  
INNER JOIN (SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS WHOL_NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  WHOL_PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) AS B  
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=B.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = B.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = B.PT_SEX_CD  
INNER JOIN (select HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, count(STATS_TRGT_COL) as STATS_TRGT_CNT from w1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) C  
ON A.HOSP_CD = C.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=C.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = C.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = C.PT_SEX_CD where C.STATS_TRGT_CNT <> 0;

FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) AS B  
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=B.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = B.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = B.PT_SEX_CD  
INNER JOIN (select HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, count(STATS_TRGT_COL) as STATS_TRGT_CNT from w1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) C  
ON A.HOSP_CD = C.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=C.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = C.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = C.PT_SEX_CD where C.STATS_TRGT_CNT <> 0;

WITH W1 AS (
SELECT A.HOSP_CD, A.PT_SBST_NO, SUBSTRING(A.DRUG_PRSC_YMD,1,4) AS CRIT_YR,  
CASE WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.DRUG_PRSC_YMD)/365.25) <'20' THEN 10 --20세 미만
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.DRUG_PRSC_YMD)/365.25) <'30' THEN 20  --20대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.DRUG_PRSC_YMD)/365.25) <'40' THEN 30  --30대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.DRUG_PRSC_YMD)/365.25) <'50' THEN 40  --40대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.DRUG_PRSC_YMD)/365.25) <'60' THEN 50  --50대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.DRUG_PRSC_YMD)/365.25) <'70' THEN 60  --60대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.DRUG_PRSC_YMD)/365.25) <'80' THEN 70  --70대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.DRUG_PRSC_YMD)/365.25)  >='80' THEN 80  --80대 이상
   END AS PT_AGE,
B.SEX AS PT_SEX_CD, A.DRUG_RXNM_NM as STATS_TRGT_COL, 
ifnull(A.DRUG_RXNM_NM,'#N/A' ) AS STATS_TRGT_VL -- NULL은 '#N/A'로 대체

ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HCODE
AND A.PT_SBST_NO = B.PTNO
AND A.DRUG_PRSC_YMD BETWEEN '20100101' AND '20211231'
)

     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ANTP_STRT_YMD)/365.25) <'60' THEN 50  --50대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ANTP_STRT_YMD)/365.25) <'70' THEN 60  --60대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ANTP_STRT_YMD)/365.25) <'80' THEN 70  --70대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ANTP_STRT_YMD)/365.25)  >='80' THEN 80  --80대 이상
   END AS PT_AGE,
B.SEX AS PT_SEX_CD, A.ANTP_LINE_CNT as STATS_TRGT_COL, 
ifnull(TO_CHAR(A.ANTP_LINE_CNT),'#N/A' ) AS STATS_TRGT_VL -- NUMERIC 컬럼 변환(NULL은 '#N/A'로 대체)
FROM GSCN_TRTM_ANTP A
INNER JOIN (SELECT DISTINCT HCODE, PTNO, ADD_DAYS(BRTH, 14) AS BRTH, SEX FROM CNCR_RGST WHERE BRTH IS NOT NULL AND POPCODE = '04' ) B -- '04'위암
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HCODE
AND A.PT_SBST_NO = B.PTNO
AND A.ANTP_STRT_YMD BETWEEN '20100101' AND '20211231'
) 
SELECT 10194 AS SMRY_STATS_NO, A.HOSP_CD, A.CRIT_YR, '위암 항암요법라인수별' AS SMRY_STATS_NM, 10210 AS TBL_ID, 1021006 AS COL_ID,
cast(A.PT_AGE as INTEGER) as PT_AGE, A.PT_SEX_CD, A.STATS_TRGT_VL, A.NCS,  B.WHOL_NCS, A.PT_CNT, B.WHOL_PT_CNT, 
TO_CHAR(CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,'YYYYMMDD') AS STATS_WORK_YMD, '20100101' AS COLL_STRT_YMD, '20211231' AS COLL_END_YMD, CURRENT_TIMESTAMP AS CRTN_DT FROM 
(SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL) AS A  
INNER JOIN (SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS WHOL_NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  WHOL_PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) AS B  
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=B.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = B.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = B.PT_SEX_CD  
INNER JOIN (select HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, count(STATS_TRGT_COL) as STATS_TRGT_CNT from w1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) C  
ON A.HOSP_CD = C.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=C.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = C.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = C.PT_SEX_CD where C.STATS_TRGT_CNT <> 0;
