(SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL) AS A  
INNER JOIN (SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS WHOL_NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  WHOL_PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) AS B  
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=B.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = B.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = B.PT_SEX_CD  
INNER JOIN (select HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, count(STATS_TRGT_COL) as STATS_TRGT_CNT from w1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) C  
ON A.HOSP_CD = C.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=C.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = C.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = C.PT_SEX_CD where C.STATS_TRGT_CNT <> 0;


-- 10200 //위암 항암요법부작용별

INSERT INTO CNCR_TBL_SMRY_STATS
(SMRY_STATS_NO, HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, SMRY_STATS_NM, TBL_ID, COL_ID, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, NCS, WHOL_NCS, PT_CNT, WHOL_PT_CNT, STATS_WORK_YMD, COLL_STRT_YMD, COLL_END_YMD, CRTN_DT) 
WITH W1 AS (
SELECT A.HOSP_CD, A.PT_SBST_NO, SUBSTRING(A.ANTP_STRT_YMD,1,4) AS CRIT_YR,  
CASE WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ANTP_STRT_YMD)/365.25) <'20' THEN 10 --20세 미만
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ANTP_STRT_YMD)/365.25) <'30' THEN 20  --20대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ANTP_STRT_YMD)/365.25) <'40' THEN 30  --30대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ANTP_STRT_YMD)/365.25) <'50' THEN 40  --40대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ANTP_STRT_YMD)/365.25) <'60' THEN 50  --50대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ANTP_STRT_YMD)/365.25) <'70' THEN 60  --60대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ANTP_STRT_YMD)/365.25) <'80' THEN 70  --70대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ANTP_STRT_YMD)/365.25)  >='80' THEN 80  --80대 이상
   END AS PT_AGE,
B.SEX AS PT_SEX_CD, A.ANTP_SEFF_CD as STATS_TRGT_COL, 
ifnull(A.ANTP_SEFF_CD,'#N/A' ) AS STATS_TRGT_VL -- NULL은 '#N/A'로 대체
FROM GSCN_TRTM_ANTP A
INNER JOIN (SELECT DISTINCT HCODE, PTNO, ADD_DAYS(BRTH, 14) AS BRTH, SEX FROM CNCR_RGST WHERE BRTH IS NOT NULL AND POPCODE = '04' ) B -- '04' 위암
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HCODE
AND A.PT_SBST_NO = B.PTNO
AND A.ANTP_STRT_YMD BETWEEN '20100101' AND '20211231'
) 
SELECT 10200 AS SMRY_STATS_NO, A.HOSP_CD, A.CRIT_YR, '위암 항암요법부작용별' AS SMRY_STATS_NM, 10210 AS TBL_ID, 1021018 AS COL_ID,
cast(A.PT_AGE as INTEGER) as PT_AGE, A.PT_SEX_CD, A.STATS_TRGT_VL, A.NCS,  B.WHOL_NCS, A.PT_CNT, B.WHOL_PT_CNT, 
TO_CHAR(CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,'YYYYMMDD') AS STATS_WORK_YMD, '20100101' AS COLL_STRT_YMD, '20211231' AS COLL_END_YMD, CURRENT_TIMESTAMP AS CRTN_DT FROM 
(SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL) AS A  
INNER JOIN (SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS WHOL_NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  WHOL_PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) AS B  
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=B.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = B.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = B.PT_SEX_CD  
INNER JOIN (select HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, count(STATS_TRGT_COL) as STATS_TRGT_CNT from w1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) C  
ON A.HOSP_CD = C.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=C.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = C.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = C.PT_SEX_CD where C.STATS_TRGT_CNT <> 0;

     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.RDT_PRSC_YMD)/365.25) <'30' THEN 20  --20대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.RDT_PRSC_YMD)/365.25) <'40' THEN 30  --30대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.RDT_PRSC_YMD)/365.25) <'50' THEN 40  --40대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.RDT_PRSC_YMD)/365.25) <'60' THEN 50  --50대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.RDT_PRSC_YMD)/365.25) <'70' THEN 60  --60대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.RDT_PRSC_YMD)/365.25) <'80' THEN 70  --70대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.RDT_PRSC_YMD)/365.25)  >='80' THEN 80  --80대 이상
   END AS PT_AGE,
B.SEX AS PT_SEX_CD, A.RDT_SMCT_CD as STATS_TRGT_COL, 
ifnull(A.RDT_SMCT_CD,'#N/A' ) AS STATS_TRGT_VL -- NULL은 '#N/A'로 대체
FROM GSCN_TRTM_RD A
INNER JOIN (SELECT DISTINCT HCODE, PTNO, ADD_DAYS(BRTH, 14) AS BRTH, SEX FROM CNCR_RGST WHERE BRTH IS NOT NULL AND POPCODE = '04' ) B -- '04' 위암
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HCODE
AND A.PT_SBST_NO = B.PTNO
AND A.RDT_PRSC_YMD BETWEEN '20100101' AND '20211231'
) 
SELECT 10205 AS SMRY_STATS_NO, A.HOSP_CD, A.CRIT_YR, '위암 방사선치료SNOMEDCT코드별' AS SMRY_STATS_NM, 10220 AS TBL_ID, 1022011 AS COL_ID,
cast(A.PT_AGE as INTEGER) as PT_AGE, A.PT_SEX_CD, A.STATS_TRGT_VL, A.NCS,  B.WHOL_NCS, A.PT_CNT, B.WHOL_PT_CNT, 
TO_CHAR(CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,'YYYYMMDD') AS STATS_WORK_YMD, '20100101' AS COLL_STRT_YMD, '20211231' AS COLL_END_YMD, CURRENT_TIMESTAMP AS CRTN_DT FROM 
(SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL) AS A  
INNER JOIN (SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS WHOL_NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  WHOL_PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) AS B  
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=B.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = B.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = B.PT_SEX_CD  
INNER JOIN (select HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, count(STATS_TRGT_COL) as STATS_TRGT_CNT from w1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) C  
ON A.HOSP_CD = C.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=C.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = C.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = C.PT_SEX_CD where C.STATS_TRGT_CNT <> 0;

cast(A.PT_AGE as INTEGER) as PT_AGE, A.PT_SEX_CD, A.STATS_TRGT_VL, A.NCS,  B.WHOL_NCS, A.PT_CNT, B.WHOL_PT_CNT, 
TO_CHAR(CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,'YYYYMMDD') AS STATS_WORK_YMD, '20100101' AS COLL_STRT_YMD, '20211231' AS COLL_END_YMD, CURRENT_TIMESTAMP AS CRTN_DT FROM 
(SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL) AS A  
INNER JOIN (SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS WHOL_NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  WHOL_PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) AS B  
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=B.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = B.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = B.PT_SEX_CD  
INNER JOIN (select HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, count(STATS_TRGT_COL) as STATS_TRGT_CNT from w1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) C  
ON A.HOSP_CD = C.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=C.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = C.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = C.PT_SEX_CD where C.STATS_TRGT_CNT <> 0;


-- 10211 //위암 부위별방사선총선량별

INSERT INTO CNCR_TBL_SMRY_STATS
(SMRY_STATS_NO, HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, SMRY_STATS_NM, TBL_ID, COL_ID, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, NCS, WHOL_NCS, PT_CNT, WHOL_PT_CNT, STATS_WORK_YMD, COLL_STRT_YMD, COLL_END_YMD, CRTN_DT) 
WITH W1 AS (
SELECT A.HOSP_CD, A.PT_SBST_NO, SUBSTRING(A.RDT_PRSC_YMD,1,4) AS CRIT_YR, 
CASE WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.RDT_PRSC_YMD)/365.25) <'20' THEN 10 --20세 미만
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.RDT_PRSC_YMD)/365.25) <'30' THEN 20  --20대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.RDT_PRSC_YMD)/365.25) <'40' THEN 30  --30대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.RDT_PRSC_YMD)/365.25) <'50' THEN 40  --40대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.RDT_PRSC_YMD)/365.25) <'60' THEN 50  --50대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.RDT_PRSC_YMD)/365.25) <'70' THEN 60  --60대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.RDT_PRSC_YMD)/365.25) <'80' THEN 70  --70대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.RDT_PRSC_YMD)/365.25)  >='80' THEN 80  --80대 이상
   END AS PT_AGE,
B.SEX AS PT_SEX_CD, A.BYST_RD_TOTL_GY as STATS_TRGT_COL, 
ifnull(TO_CHAR(A.BYST_RD_TOTL_GY),'#N/A' ) AS STATS_TRGT_VL -- NUMERIC 컬럼 변환(NULL은 '#N/A'로 대체)
FROM GSCN_TRTM_RD A
INNER JOIN (SELECT DISTINCT HCODE, PTNO, ADD_DAYS(BRTH, 14) AS BRTH, SEX FROM CNCR_RGST WHERE BRTH IS NOT NULL AND POPCODE = '04' ) B -- '04'위암
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HCODE
AND A.PT_SBST_NO = B.PTNO
AND A.RDT_PRSC_YMD BETWEEN '20100101' AND '20211231'
) 
SELECT 10211 AS SMRY_STATS_NO, A.HOSP_CD, A.CRIT_YR, '위암 부위별방사선총선량별' AS SMRY_STATS_NM, 10220 AS TBL_ID, 1022019 AS COL_ID,

TO_CHAR(CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,'YYYYMMDD') AS STATS_WORK_YMD, '20100101' AS COLL_STRT_YMD, '20211231' AS COLL_END_YMD, CURRENT_TIMESTAMP AS CRTN_DT FROM 
(SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL) AS A  
INNER JOIN (SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS WHOL_NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  WHOL_PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) AS B  
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=B.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = B.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = B.PT_SEX_CD  
INNER JOIN (select HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, count(STATS_TRGT_COL) as STATS_TRGT_CNT from w1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) C

-- 10216 //위암 재발진단방법별

INSERT INTO CNCR_TBL_SMRY_STATS
(SMRY_STATS_NO, HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, SMRY_STATS_NM, TBL_ID, COL_ID, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, NCS, WHOL_NCS, PT_CNT, WHOL_PT_CNT, STATS_WORK_YMD, COLL_STRT_YMD, COLL_END_YMD, CRTN_DT) 
WITH W1 AS (
SELECT A.HOSP_CD, A.PT_SBST_NO, SUBSTRING(A.RLDG_YMD,1,4) AS CRIT_YR,  
CASE WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.RLDG_YMD)/365.25) <'20' THEN 10 --20세 미만
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.RLDG_YMD)/365.25) <'30' THEN 20  --20대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.RLDG_YMD)/365.25) <'40' THEN 30  --30대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.RLDG_YMD)/365.25) <'50' THEN 40  --40대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.RLDG_YMD)/365.25) <'60' THEN 50  --50대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.RLDG_YMD)/365.25) <'70' THEN 60  --60대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.RLDG_YMD)/365.25) <'80' THEN 70  --70대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.RLDG_YMD)/365.25)  >='80' THEN 80  --80대 이상
   END AS PT_AGE,
B.SEX AS PT_SEX_CD, A.RLDG_MTCD as STATS_TRGT_COL, 
ifnull(A.RLDG_MTCD,'#N/A' ) AS STATS_TRGT_VL -- NULL은 '#N/A'로 대체
FROM GSCN_FUOR_RLPS A
INNER JOIN (SELECT DISTINCT HCODE, PTNO, ADD_DAYS(BRTH, 14) AS BRTH, SEX FROM CNCR_RGST WHERE BRTH IS NOT NULL AND POPCODE = '04' ) B -- '04' 위암
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HCODE
AND A.PT_SBST_NO = B.PTNO
AND A.RLDG_YMD BETWEEN '20100101' AND '20211231'
) 
SELECT 10216 AS SMRY_STATS_NO, A.HOSP_CD, A.CRIT_YR, '위암 재발진단방법별' AS SMRY_STATS_NM, 10230 AS TBL_ID, 1023005 AS COL_ID,
cast(A.PT_AGE as INTEGER) as PT_AGE, A.PT_SEX_CD, A.STATS_TRGT_VL, A.NCS,  B.WHOL_NCS, A.PT_CNT, B.WHOL_PT_CNT, 
TO_CHAR(CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,'YYYYMMDD') AS STATS_WORK_YMD, '20100101' AS COLL_STRT_YMD, '20211231' AS COLL_END_YMD, CURRENT_TIMESTAMP AS CRTN_DT FROM 
(SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL) AS A  
INNER JOIN (SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS WHOL_NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  WHOL_PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) AS B  
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=B.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = B.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = B.PT_SEX_CD  
INNER JOIN (select HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, count(STATS_TRGT_COL) as STATS_TRGT_CNT from w1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) C  
ON A.HOSP_CD = C.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=C.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = C.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = C.PT_SEX_CD where C.STATS_TRGT_CNT <> 0;


-- 10217 //위암 재발부위별

INSERT INTO CNCR_TBL_SMRY_STATS
(SMRY_STATS_NO, HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, SMRY_STATS_NM, TBL_ID, COL_ID, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, NCS, WHOL_NCS, PT_CNT, WHOL_PT_CNT, STATS_WORK_YMD, COLL_STRT_YMD, COLL_END_YMD, CRTN_DT) 
WITH W1 AS (
SELECT A.HOSP_CD, A.PT_SBST_NO, SUBSTRING(A.RLDG_YMD,1,4) AS CRIT_YR,  
CASE WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.RLDG_YMD)/365.25) <'20' THEN 10 --20세 미만
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.RLDG_YMD)/365.25) <'30' THEN 20  --20대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.RLDG_YMD)/365.25) <'40' THEN 30  --30대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.RLDG_YMD)/365.25) <'50' THEN 40  --40대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.RLDG_YMD)/365.25) <'60' THEN 50  --50대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.RLDG_YMD)/365.25) <'70' THEN 60  --60대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.RLDG_YMD)/365.25) <'80' THEN 70  --70대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.RLDG_YMD)/365.25)  >='80' THEN 80  --80대 이상
   END AS PT_AGE,
B.SEX AS PT_SEX_CD, A.RLPS_SITE_CD as STATS_TRGT_COL, 
ifnull(A.RLPS_SITE_CD,'#N/A' ) AS STATS_TRGT_VL -- NULL은 '#N/A'로 대체
FROM GSCN_FUOR_RLPS A
INNER JOIN (SELECT DISTINCT HCODE, PTNO, ADD_DAYS(BRTH, 14) AS BRTH, SEX FROM CNCR_RGST WHERE BRTH IS NOT NULL AND POPCODE = '04' ) B -- '04' 위암
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HCODE
AND A.PT_SBST_NO = B.PTNO
AND A.RLDG_YMD BETWEEN '20100101' AND '20211231'
) 
SELECT 10217 AS SMRY_STATS_NO, A.HOSP_CD, A.CRIT_YR, '위암 재발부위별' AS SMRY_STATS_NM, 10230 AS TBL_ID, 1023007 AS COL_ID,
cast(A.PT_AGE as INTEGER) as PT_AGE, A.PT_SEX_CD, A.STATS_TRGT_VL, A.NCS,  B.WHOL_NCS, A.PT_CNT, B.WHOL_PT_CNT, 
TO_CHAR(CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,'YYYYMMDD') AS STATS_WORK_YMD, '20100101' AS COLL_STRT_YMD, '20211231' AS COLL_END_YMD, CURRENT_TIMESTAMP AS CRTN_DT FROM 
(SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL) AS A  
INNER JOIN (SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS WHOL_NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  WHOL_PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) AS B  
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=B.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = B.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = B.PT_SEX_CD  
INNER JOIN (select HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, count(STATS_TRGT_COL) as STATS_TRGT_CNT from w1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) C  
ON A.HOSP_CD = C.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=C.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = C.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = C.PT_SEX_CD where C.STATS_TRGT_CNT <> 0;


-- 10218 //위암 재발종류별

INSERT INTO CNCR_TBL_SMRY_STATS
(SMRY_STATS_NO, HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, SMRY_STATS_NM, TBL_ID, COL_ID, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, NCS, WHOL_NCS, PT_CNT, WHOL_PT_CNT, STATS_WORK_YMD, COLL_STRT_YMD, COLL_END_YMD, CRTN_DT) 
WITH W1 AS (

     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.RLDG_YMD)/365.25) <'50' THEN 40  --40대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.RLDG_YMD)/365.25) <'60' THEN 50  --50대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.RLDG_YMD)/365.25) <'70' THEN 60  --60대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.RLDG_YMD)/365.25) <'80' THEN 70  --70대

AND A.PT_SBST_NO = B.PTNO
AND A.RLDG_YMD BETWEEN '20100101' AND '20211231'

TO_CHAR(CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,'YYYYMMDD') AS STATS_WORK_YMD, '20100101' AS COLL_STRT_YMD, '20211231' AS COLL_END_YMD, CURRENT_TIMESTAMP AS CRTN_DT FROM

FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL) AS A  
INNER JOIN (SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS WHOL_NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  WHOL_PT_CNT
